PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 6
Question 1 of 200
Question ID: 612661
In an effort to get your new project team to be as cohesive as possible, you have been conducting
a series of on-site team-building activities. You believe that your efforts have helped team
members improve both their interpersonal relationships and the level of trust in the team.
What should you do next to determine if your efforts have been successful?
- **A Monitor the team engagement matrix**
- **B Develop a team charter**
- **C Conduct team performance assessments**
- **D Create a responsibility assignment matrix (RAM)**
Correct Answer: C

**Hint:**

After implementing team development efforts, how would you determine if they have been
successful?

**Explanation:**

The scenario implies the project manager is carrying out the Develop Team process. Team
performance assessments are an output of that process. Ongoing team performance assessments
give the project manager insight into whether the team development efforts such as team
building, which is a tool of the Develop team process, have been effective. As initiatives such as
training and team building are implemented, the project manager should see improvements in the
team's effectiveness and cohesiveness. The correct team development strategies and activities
will increase the team's performance, which, in turn, increases the likelihood of meeting project
objectives. Therefore, in the scenario described, making a team performance assessment is the
next step to take and is the best way to determine if the team building efforts have been
productive.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Monitor the team engagement matrix**
Incorrect. The 'team engagement matrix' is a fake term made-up for this question.
- **B Develop a team charter**
Incorrect. The team charter is a document developed as part of the Plan Resource
Management process that establishes the team values, agreements, and operating
guidelines for the team. The team charter does not assess team-building activities.
- **C Conduct team performance assessments**
Correct. As initiatives such as training and team building are implemented, the project
manager should see improvements in the team's effectiveness. Making a team performance
assessment would be the best way to determine if the team building efforts, performed in
this scenario, have been effective.
- **D Create a responsibility assignment matrix (RAM)**
Incorrect. A RAM shows the project resources assigned to each work package. It is used to
illustrate the connections between work packages, or activities, and project team members.
The RAM does not have any utility in assessing team-building.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 341, 343
Live FeedbackTM Back to Results
Next

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 6
Question 2 of 200
Question ID: 612841
- **A project manager is in the process of monitoring costs for a hotel construction project and**
determines that the project is running over budget with a 10% deviation from the baseline plan.
What should the project manager do to determine if corrective action is necessary?
- **A Perform the Plan Cost Management plan to develop the control thresholds**
- **B Review the cost register to find the triggers for corrective actions**
- **C Check the cost management plan for a variance threshold**
- **D Speak with the PMO for guidance on the implementation of corrective actions**
Correct Answer: C

**Hint:**

An element of the project management plan should have information on control thresholds.

**Explanation:**

The question implies that the Control Costs process is being performed. The cost management
plan is one of the inputs into the Control Costs process and is the component of a project
management plan that describes how costs will be planned, structured, and controlled including
any established control thresholds. The variance thresholds for monitoring cost performance may
indicate an agreed-upon amount of variation to be allowed before some action needs to be taken.
Thresholds are typically expressed as percentage deviations from the baseline plan. Therefore, of
the available options, checking the cost management plan for a variance threshold is the best
answer to the question asked.

**Details for Each Option:**


---

- **A Perform the Plan Cost Management plan to develop the control thresholds**
Incorrect. The question suggests that the project manager is conducting the Control Costs
process. One of the primary inputs to this process is the cost management plan which is
produced earlier in the project as part of the Plan Cost Management process. The cost
management plan should have the relevant information regarding the control thresholds for
the project. Therefore, there is no reason to perform the Plan Cost Management process to
develop control thresholds when that information should already be available in the cost
management plan.
- **B Review the cost register to find the triggers for corrective actions**
Incorrect. 'Cost register' is a fake term made up for this question.
- **C Check the cost management plan for a variance threshold**
Correct. The cost management plan describes how costs will be planned, structured, and
controlled including any established control thresholds. The variance thresholds may
include an agreed-upon amount of variation to be allowed before action needs to be taken.
- **D Speak with the PMO for guidance on the implementation of corrective actions**
Incorrect. The question does not state whether or not the performing organization utilizes a
project management office (PMO). Regardless, the PMO may or may not have detailed
information about controlling costs for a given project. However, there is no reason to ask
the PMO for guidance when the information should be readily available in the project
management plan.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 239, 259

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 6
Question 3 of 200
Question ID: 612209
- **A project aims to provide each sales associate with a tablet to use for sales and other**
transactions. During a trial to test the functionality of the system, the team discovers that the
Wi-Fi coverage is inadequate in certain parts of the store.
What should be done first?
- **A Discuss the problem in the next status review meeting**
- **B Assess the financial implications of the problem**
- **C Submit a change request to update the schedule baseline**
- **D Update the project documents**
Correct Answer: D

**Hint:**

Where is information about problems encountered during a project recorded and monitored?

**Explanation:**

The issue log is a project document, where information about issues is recorded and monitored.
The issue log should be updated immediately to include details of the Wi-Fi issue, so the
problem can be effectively tracked, assigned an owner, and monitored to ensure a resolution. In
addition to the issue log, the risk register, lessons learned register, and possibly other project
documents may also be updated. However, the first thing the project manager should do in this
situation is to update the issue log. The issue log was not specifically listed as an answer choice,
but it is an example of a project document. Updating the project documents, which includes the
issue log, is the best answer to the question asked.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Discuss the problem in the next status review meeting**
Incorrect. Although the problem may be a valid topic for discussion in the next status
review meeting, the project manager should not wait until the next status review meeting to
take action. The problem should be immediately recorded in the issue log.
- **B Assess the financial implications of the problem**
Incorrect. Once the root cause of the issue is understood, an assessment can be made to
determine the cost to resolve the issue. However, the Wi-Fi coverage issue should first be
captured in the issue log.
- **C Submit a change request to update the schedule baseline**
Incorrect. While the project manager may have to go through the change request process to
update the schedule baseline, that determination cannot be made until the problem is
analyzed and implications are understood.
- **D Update the project documents**
Correct. The issue log is a project document that should be updated immediately to include
details of the Wi-Fi issue, so the problem can be effectively tracked and monitored to ensure
a resolution.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 458
Live FeedbackTM Back to Results

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 6
Question 4 of 200
Question ID: 612881
Working for a manufacturing company as a project manager, you are in the process of defining
and documenting stakeholders' needs for a new product development project. You have decided
to use a facilitation technique known as quality function deployment (QFD).
What should you do first when applying this technique?
- **A Create a context diagram to serve as a visual depiction of the product scope**
- **B Build a prototype to obtain early feedback on requirements**
- **C Review the requirements documentation in order to prepare for the QFD**
- **D Use the voice of the customer (VOC) to gather customer needs**
Correct Answer: D

**Hint:**

QFD is a facilitation technique that helps determine the critical characteristics for new product
development.

**Explanation:**

The question implies that you, as the project manager, are currently performing the Collect
Requirements process. In the manufacturing industry, quality function deployment (QFD) is a
facilitation technique that helps determine the critical characteristics for new product
development. QFD starts by collecting customer needs, also known as the voice of the customer
(VOC). These needs are then objectively sorted and prioritized, and goals are set for achieving
them. Therefore, of the available choices, using the voice of the customer (VOC) to gather
customer needs is what you should do first.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Create a context diagram to serve as a visual depiction of the product scope**
Incorrect. A context diagram is a visual depiction of the product scope showing a business
system (process, equipment, computer system, etc.), and how people and other systems
(actors) interact with it. Although a context diagram is a tool that may be useful during the
Collect Requirements process, it is not related to a facilitation technique as requested by
the question.
- **B Build a prototype to obtain early feedback on requirements**
Incorrect. A prototype can be used as a method of obtaining early feedback on
requirements by providing a working model of the expected product before actually
building it. However, the first step with QFD is to collect customer needs rather than
building a prototype.
- **C Review the requirements documentation in order to prepare for the QFD**
Incorrect. The question suggests that you, as the project manager, are conducting the
Collect Requirements process. The requirements documentation is an output of the Collect
Requirements process. Therefore, the customer needs must first be determined before the
requirements documentation can be created.
- **D Use the voice of the customer (VOC) to gather customer needs**
Correct. QFD starts by collecting customer needs, also known as the voice of the customer
(VOC). These needs are then objectively sorted and prioritized, and goals are set for
achieving them.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 145

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 6
Question 5 of 200
Question ID: 613624
You were recently hired by an electrical engineering firm to take over as the project manager for
the installation of backup generators in a religious community. When reviewing the project
schedule, you notice that several holidays that are observed by the community were not
accounted for.
What would be the first project document that you would add the community's observed holidays
to as non-working days?
- **A Master schedule**
- **B Project calendar**
- **C Duration estimates**
- **D Resource calendar**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

What is an output of the Develop Schedule process that accounts for non-working days?
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

The project calendar is originally an organizational process asset (OPA) that is updated according
to project activities and is an output of the Develop Schedule process. As the project manager,
you would reference the project calendar specific to the project to determine the working days
and shifts that are available for scheduled activities. The project calendar is specific to the
project, and it takes into account all the constraints of the project, such as observed holidays of
the client.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Master schedule**
Incorrect. The master schedule, also known as the milestone schedule, is a summary-level
project schedule that identifies the major deliverables and work breakdown components
and key schedule milestones. Although the non-working days would be incorporated into
the project schedule (and therefore accounted for in the master schedule), they would first
need to be acknowledged and added to the project calendar.
- **B Project calendar**
Correct. The project calendar identifies the working days and shifts that are available for
scheduled activities. Project calendars distinguish time periods in days or parts of days that
are available to complete scheduled activities from time periods that are not available for
work.
- **C Duration estimates**
Incorrect. Duration estimates provide the amount of time each activity will take to
complete. Duration estimates take into account the non-working days, but the non-working
days have no bearing on the number of scheduled hours it takes to complete an activity.
- **D Resource calendar**
Incorrect. The resource calendar identifies the working days and shifts upon which each
specific resource (e.g., a team member or equipment) is available. Resource calendars
show when resources are in use or not in use, which may make the resource available for
other projects. They do not identify the specific project's non-working days.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 220
Live FeedbackTM Back to Results

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 6
Question 6 of 200
Question ID: 613299
- **A project to build a new generation nuclear reactor to power a small city has just started. The**
public is divided on the project. While many have no concerns, some are worried about safety,
and others think it will have cost overruns.
How should the project manager deal with communicating the potential risks and issues?
- **A Describe the information sharing process with the public in the communications**
management plan.
- **B Risks and issues are internal to the project and do not need to be communicated outside**
the project.
- **C Invite the public representatives to the daily standup meetings with the project team.**
- **D Make the risk register and issue log a public document for the sake of transparency.**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

All stakeholders need to know about the risks and issues.
Correct Answer: A

**Explanation:**

The communications management plan is a component of the project management plan that
describes how project communications will be planned, structured, implemented, and monitored
for effectiveness. This plan is the main output of the Plan Communications Management process.
Guideance on how project information, including the risks and issues, should be shared
internally as well as externally with stakeholders, including the general public, should be part of
the communications management plan. Therefore, of the choices provided, describing the

---

information sharing process with the public in the communications management plan is the best
answer to the question asked.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Describe the information sharing process with the public in the communications**
management plan.
Correct. The communications management plan should outline the process of information
sharing with both internal and external stakeholders.
- **B Risks and issues are internal to the project and do not need to be communicated outside**
the project.
Incorrect. Public projects typically require transparency with the public whenever possible.
Besides, without public support, the project will likely fail. Hence there needs to be some
degree of communication of the issues and risks to the public.
- **C Invite the public representatives to the daily standup meetings with the project team.**
Incorrect. Inviting the public representatives to the daily standup meetings with the project
team sounds unrealistic and unnecessary. There are more effective ways to keep the public
informed.
- **D Make the risk register and issue log a public document for the sake of transparency.**
Incorrect. Not everyone is well versed in the project management language, and making the
risk register and the issue log public would likely lead to misinterpretation. Additionally,
there may be sensitive and confidential information contained in these documents which
should not be shared with the public.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 377
Live FeedbackTM Back to Results

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 6
Question 7 of 200
Question ID: 613245
An inspection of a shipbuilding project has identified consistent welding failures in critical
components resulting in substantial rework, schedule delays, and budget overruns. A quality
management team has been tasked to identify the root cause of the problem. The team has
determined that inadequate welder training was the predominant reason.
What should the project manager do next?
- **A Request an audit by the enterprise quality team to confirm the root causes of the issue, its**
impact on the project, and the cost of future rework.
- **B Request extra budget money to cover the cost of the welding rework and additional**
inspection teams.
- **C Determine training options and prepare a quality report with a summary of the issue and**
recommendations for corrective actions.
- **D Meet with the welders to emphasize that the quality of work is unacceptable and that**
future failures will result in disciplinary action.
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Which answer is both proactive and positive?
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

This scenario implies that the project manager performs the Manage Quality process. The
problem and its root cause have been identified, so it is time to determine options and make
recommendations. Quality reports are an output of the Manage Quality process, and they are the
best way to include a summary of findings, potential options, and recommendations. The key
here is to find a path forward that will correct the problem in a positive, proactive way. Since the

---

inadequate welder training was the predominant reason, of the choices provided, determining
training options and preparing a quality report with a summary of the issue and recommendations
for corrective actions is what the project manager should do next.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Request an audit by the enterprise quality team to confirm the root causes of the issue, its**
impact on the project, and the cost of future rework.
Incorrect. The issue and its root cause have already been identified. Therefore, requesting
an audit to confirm the root cause is a waste of time and resources. Now it's time for the
project manager to make recommendations for corrective action.
- **B Request extra budget money to cover the cost of the welding rework and additional**
inspection teams.
Incorrect. The cost of rework is usually much higher than the cost of prevention.
Additionally, this approach will allow the substandard work to continue, potentially
resulting in more failures.
- **C Determine training options and prepare a quality report with a summary of the issue and**
recommendations for corrective actions.
Correct. The project manager is expected to be proactive and make recommendations for
corrective actions. In this case, a quality report is the best way to ensure that identified
quality issues are addressed.
- **D Meet with the welders to emphasize that the quality of work is unacceptable and that**
future failures will result in disciplinary action.
Incorrect. The problem has been identified as an inadequate training issue, so demanding
higher quality work from an improperly trained workforce will be counterproductive.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page 296
Live FeedbackTM Back to Results

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 6
Question 8 of 200
Question ID: 612884
- **A project manager has taken extra care to identify dozens of individual activity risks on the**
project and has established reserves for the identified risks. During the gate review to start the
execution stage of the project, the steering committee does not approve the project to proceed to
execution due to inadequate reserves.
What did the project manager most likely forget to do?
- **A Look at overall project risk**
- **B Establish management reserves for each identified risk**
- **C Correctly estimate activity costs**
- **D Assign control accounts to the reserves**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

What type of risk has the project manager neglected to consider?
Correct Answer: A

**Explanation:**

Contingency reserves are represented by the time or money allocated in the schedule or cost
baseline for known risks with active response strategies. In this scenario, it appears that the
project manager has accounted for the individual project risks with contingency reserves.
Contingency reserves are associated with the project’s known-unknowns, and these reserves are
under the project manager's control. However, it does not appear that the project manager
considered overall project risks and unknown project risks, sometimes referred to as
unknown-unknowns. These risks are addressed with management reserves. The management
reserve is an amount of the project budget or project schedule held outside of the performance
measurement baseline (PMB) for management control purposes, that is reserved for unforeseen

---

work that is within the scope of the project. Had the project manager considered overall project
risk, the appropriate management reserves would likely have been established, and the project
may not have been halted due to a lack of reserves.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Look at overall project risk**
Correct. Individual activity risks look only at tasks. Overall project risks account for risks
that are broader in scope than just the activities.
- **B Establish management reserves for each identified risk**
Incorrect. Contingency reserves, not management reserves, are established to address
identified risks. Management reserves are set aside to address overall project risks and as
well as unknown risks.
- **C Correctly estimate activity costs**
Incorrect. Based on the scenario, there is no indication that the activity costs are incorrect.
The question states that the project is being halted due to inadequate reserves rather than
activity costs.
- **D Assign control accounts to the reserves**
Incorrect. A control account is a management control point where scope, budget, actual
cost, and schedule are integrated and compared to the earned value for performance
measurement. Control accounts are assigned to work packages and not to individual risks
or their reserves.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 254-255
Live FeedbackTM Back to Results
Prev Next

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 6
Question 9 of 200
Question ID: 612697
One month into a project, the project manager is pleased to see the plans are working well. One
morning the project manager gets an email from the accounting department saying the project is
performing poorly. After some investigation, the project manager determines that neither the
costs nor the resource utilization numbers have been updated in the corporate accounting system.
What is the most likely problem?
- **A Improper reporting formats**
- **B Incorrect organizational procedures links**
- **C Rules of performance measurement**
- **D Improper control thresholds**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

What connects the project to the corporate accounting system?
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

The work breakdown structure (WBS) component used for the project cost accounting is called
the control account. Each control account is assigned a unique code or account number(s) that
links directly to the performing organization's accounting system. Thus, these organizational
process links keep the corporate accounting system up to date and consistent with the project's
actual performance. If the organizational procedures links are defined incorrectly, project and
corporate systems will not match, which may lead to the project manager having a vastly
different view of project performance than the accounting department. Therefore, of the available

---

options, "incorrect organizational procedures links" is the most likely cause of the problem
described by the question.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Improper reporting formats**
Incorrect. The format and frequency for the various cost reports are defined in the cost
management plan. However, the question suggests that accurate cost reports are available
as the project manager is pleased with the project's results thus far, making improper
reporting formats an unlikely source of the problem. Even if the cost reports were flawed,
this would be an indirect cause of the problem, and there is another answer choice that
directly links project costs to the performing organization's accounting system.
- **B Incorrect organizational procedures links**
Correct. If the organizational procedures links are defined incorrectly, the project
performance and corporate accounting system will not match, which may lead to the
project manager having a vastly different view of project performance than the accounting
department.
- **C Rules of performance measurement**
Incorrect. Although the measurement points for control accounts in the WBS are defined in
the rules of performance measurement, the project manager sees that the project’s reports
are being updated but are just not being updated in the corporate accounting system.
Hence, the rules of performance are not likely to be an issue.
- **D Improper control thresholds**
Incorrect. Control thresholds may be included in the cost management plan to indicate the
allowable variance from the baseline. Improper control accounts, not control thresholds,
might account for the problem described in the question.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 239
Live FeedbackTM Back to Results

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 6
Question 10 of 200
Question ID: 612253
Reserve analysis indicates that the remaining contingency reserves of a project are insufficient to
cover the cost of implementing the risk responses that are currently underway. However, the
existing management reserves should be adequate to cover the immediate need, as well as the
remaining risk in the project.
What is the best course of action in this situation?
- **A Submit a change request to access the contingency reserves**
- **B Ask the project sponsor to increase the project budget**
- **C Submit a change request to transfer the management reserves into the cost baseline**
- **D Use the existing management reserves as needed since they are included in the project**
budget
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Management reserves are not included in the cost baseline.
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

- **A reserve analysis may be performed as part of the Monitor Risks process. The question**
indicates that the current contingency reserves are insufficient to cover the current need, but the
management reserves are still adequate for the risk responses currently being implemented and
the remaining project risk. Contingency reserves are included in the cost baseline, and the project
manager has direct control over these funds. The management reserves are part of the overall
project budget but are not included in the cost baseline. The project manager only has access to
the funds in the cost baseline. In this case, an approved change request is required to transfer the
funds from the management reserves into the cost baseline. Once the funds from management

---

reserves have been released, the project manager can access the funds as part of the cost baseline.
Therefore, of the available options, the best course of action for the project manager is to submit
a change request to transfer the management reserves into the cost baseline.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Submit a change request to access the contingency reserves**
Incorrect. Contingency reserves are part of the cost baseline and can be accessed by the
project manager without affecting the cost baseline. Therefore, an approved change request
is not required to access the contingency reserves. Additionally, the question states that the
remaining contingency reserves will be insufficient to address the risk responses currently
underway.
- **B Ask the project sponsor to increase the project budget**
Incorrect. Based on the information provided, the budget is adequate, and the management
reserves (which are part of the budget) are expected to cover the remaining project risk.
Should it be required at some later point, a budget increase may be requested through the
formal change request process.
- **C Submit a change request to transfer the management reserves into the cost baseline**
Correct. An approved change request is required to transfer the funds from management
reserves into the cost baseline. Once the funds from management reserves have been
released, the project manager can access the funds as part of the cost baseline.
- **D Use the existing management reserves as needed since they are included in the project**
budget
Incorrect. Management reserves are part of the overall project budget but are not included
in the cost baseline. An approved change request is required to transfer the management
reserves into the cost baseline for the project manager to access these funds.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 254-255, 457
Live FeedbackTM Back to Results
Prev Next

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 6
Question 11 of 200
Question ID: 612186
You have completed the process of creating the work breakdown structure (WBS).
What should you do next?
- **A Develop the scope baseline**
- **B Create the network diagram**
- **C Create an activity list**
- **D Determine the critical path**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Decomposition of the WBS will lead to this project document.
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

After finishing the WBS, the next process would be Define Activities where the WBS is
decomposed into activities that are small enough to estimate, schedule, monitor, and control
resulting in an activity list. However, the question is not asking what 'process' should be
performed next. The question is asking 'What should you do next?' after you have completed the
process of creating the WBS. An activity list is one of the outputs from the Define Activities
process. Therefore, creating an activity list is what you should do next, making that action the
best answer to the question asked.

**Details for Each Option:**


---

- **A Develop the scope baseline**
Incorrect. The scope baseline includes the scope statement, WBS, WBS dictionary, work
packages, and planning packages. The scope baseline is an output of the Create WBS
process, which, according to the scenario, you have just completed.
- **B Create the network diagram**
Incorrect. The network diagram is a graphical representation of the logical relationships
among the project schedule activities. The work packages from the WBS are decomposed
into activities, and then the activities are sequenced before the network diagram can be
created. In the scenario described, only the WBS has been created, and no further
decomposition has occurred. Therefore, you have not progressed far enough in the project
planning to create a network diagram.
- **C Create an activity list**
Correct. The work packages of the WBS are decomposed further into the activities that are
required to produce the work package deliverables in the Define Activities process. An
activities list is the output of the Define Activities process making this the correct answer.
- **D Determine the critical path**
Incorrect. The critical path is the sequence of activities that represents the longest path
through a project, which determines the project's shortest possible duration. It is a tool
used to develop the schedule. To determine the critical path, the WBS has to be decomposed
further into activities, the activities sequenced, and a network diagram created. Having
only finished the WBS in this scenario, you are not ready to determine the critical path yet.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 183
Live FeedbackTM Back to Results
Prev Next

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 6
Question 12 of 200
Question ID: 612683
- **A project manager is leading a project with high levels of uncertainty and unpredictability. As a**
result, the project manager has spent an inordinate amount of time dealing with a large volume of
change requests, which have put the project significantly behind schedule.
What could the project manager have done differently to control the schedule better?
- **A Used iterative scheduling with a backlog**
- **B Authorized a change control board (CCB)**
- **C Applied a waterfall framework to the project**
- **D Further decomposed of the WBS before the start of the project**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

What type of project management framework is better suited to a project with an evolving
project scope?
Correct Answer: A

**Explanation:**

High levels of uncertainty and unpredictability make long-term scope difficult to define.
Adaptive planning defines a plan but acknowledges that once work starts, the priorities may
change and that the plan may need to be updated. One of the trends and emerging practices for
Project Schedule Management includes iterative scheduling with a backlog. Iterative scheduling
is a form of rolling wave planning based on adaptive life cycles, such as the agile approach for
product development. The requirements are documented in user stories that are then prioritized
and refined just prior to construction, and the product features are developed using time-boxed
periods of work. The benefit of this approach is that it welcomes changes throughout the
development life cycle and may reduce or eliminate the need for a formal change control

---

process. Therefore, of the available choices, using iterative scheduling with a backlog is the best
answer to the question asked.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Used iterative scheduling with a backlog**
Correct. Iterative scheduling is a form of rolling wave planning based on adaptive life
cycles, such as the agile approach for product development. The benefit of this approach is
that it welcomes changes throughout the development life cycle and may reduce or
eliminate the need for a formal change control process.
- **B Authorized a change control board (CCB)**
Incorrect. A change control board (CCB) is a formally chartered group responsible for
reviewing, evaluating, approving, delaying, or rejecting changes to the project. However,
the question describes a situation, where the uncertainty of the project has led to excessive
change requests, and just changing how the requests are reviewed and approved does not
affect the volume of change requests.
- **C Applied a waterfall framework to the project**
Incorrect. A waterfall or traditional project management approach is one in which the
project is thoroughly planned before project execution begins. A waterfall framework may
not be appropriate for a project with a great deal of unpredictability and change.
Additionally, the large volume of change requests suggests that a waterfall methodology is
being used in this scenario.
- **D Further decomposed of the WBS before the start of the project**
Incorrect. A work breakdown structure (WBS) is a hierarchical decomposition of the total
scope of work to be carried out by the project team to accomplish the project objectives and
create the required deliverables. Detailed project planning, including the decomposition of
the WBS, is problematic for a project with a great deal of unpredictability and change. The
WBS would need to be modified with each successive change to the project scope. A
detailed WBS would not address the problems associated with evolving project scope.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 177

---

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 6
Question 13 of 200
Question ID: 613366
You are leading a software development project, which requires knowledge of several
programming languages. During project execution, one of the developers has been pulled out of
the project by her functional manager. The manager provided you with another developer
instead.
What should you do first?
- **A Provide the new developer with an ability test**
- **B Introduce the new developer to the project sponsor**
- **C Schedule training for the new developer**
- **D Assign the developer the next user story in the backlog**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

How might you evaluate the new developer's current skill set?
Correct Answer: A

**Explanation:**

Individual and team assessments are tools that may be useful in the Develop Team process.
Individual and team assessment tools give the project manager and the project team insight into
areas of strengths and weaknesses. These tools help project managers assess team members'
preferences, aspirations, how they process and organize information, how they make decisions,
and how they interact with people. Various tools are available such as attitudinal surveys,
specific assessments, structured interviews, ability tests, and focus groups. An ability test would
provide an assessment of the new developer's existing competencies in order to determine what,
if any, gaps in skill set exist and how they might be addressed. The incorrect answer choices
represent actions which are premature without understanding the new developer's existing

---

competencies. Of the available options, providing the new developer with an ability test to
evaluate the developer's existing competencies is what you, as the project manager should do
first.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Provide the new developer with an ability test**
Correct. An ability test would provide an assessment of the new developer's existing
competencies in order to determine what, if any, gaps in skill set exist and how they might
be addressed.
- **B Introduce the new developer to the project sponsor**
Incorrect. It is unlikely that introducing the new developer to the project sponsor should be
your first step in this situation. Bringing the new developer up to speed to perform the
project work is more important. The developer's skills should be assessed to understand
what training, if any, is required.
- **C Schedule training for the new developer**
Incorrect. The new developer may or may not need additional training for the current
project. You, as the project manager, should perform an individual assessment of the new
developers existing skillset to determine if training is necessary, and, if so, which training
options would be the most beneficial in closing any knowledge gaps.
- **D Assign the developer the next user story in the backlog**
Incorrect. The new developer may or may not have the required competencies to complete
the next user story successfully. You, as the project manager, should first gain an
understanding of the new developer's skill set to determine if the next user story is an
appropriate assignment for the developer. Failing to take this step, may set the new
developer up for failure.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 342

PMP Exam 6
Question 14 of 200
Question ID: 612106
Email has been used on a project to communicate with stakeholders. Midway through project
execution, a project manager learns about a social media platform that has been proven more
effective with stakeholder engagement.
To begin using the new platform, what should the project manager do first?
- **A Update the communications management plan**
- **B Submit a change request**
- **C Revise the stakeholder engagement plan**
- **D Start using the social media site as needed**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Any change to the project management plan goes through the organization's change control
process.
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

The scenario describes a project in the execution stage. The project manager wants to change the
method used to communicate with some of the project stakeholders. Methods or technologies
used to convey the information, such as memos, email, press releases, or social media are
included in the communications management plan. Any change to the project management plan
or its subsidiaries needs to go through the organization's change control process which begins
with a change request. Therefore, after the project manager decides to use the corporate social
media site for some communications on her project, she needs to issue a change request to make
the necessary updates to the communications management plan.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Update the communications management plan**
Incorrect. The project is in execution implying the project management plan has been
approved. Any change to the approved project management plan, or one of its components,
requires going through the organization's change control process via a change request. The
communications management plan will require an update to reflect the use of the corporate
social media site as a method for distributing project communications. However, to update
the communications management plan, an approved change request is required first.
- **B Submit a change request**
Correct. The communications management plan will require an update to reflect the use of
the corporate social media site as a method for distributing project communications.
However, any change to the project management plan or any of its components requires
utilizing the organization's change control process which begins with issuing a change
request.
- **C Revise the stakeholder engagement plan**
Incorrect. The stakeholder engagement plan describes how to promote the productive
involvement of stakeholders in a project. While this plan may need to be updated, the
update cannot be done at will. A change request should be submitted first.
- **D Start using the social media site as needed**
Incorrect. The project is in the execution stage, meaning the communications are managed
according to the communications management plan. Changing communication methods
during project execution, for example, by switching from email to social media, should be
handled according to the organization’s change control process which begins by submitting
a change request. Therefore, the project manager cannot start using the social media site
for communications until she has approval for the change.

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 96-97, 377

Question 15 of 200
Question ID: 612332
Your company has initiated a new project to implement a project management office within the
company and has assigned you as the project manager. You have been asked to draft a project
charter but you have very little experience managing projects and are unsure how to create a
project charter.
Which of the following would be the most important item you will need to complete this task?
- **A The integration plan**
- **B The project management plan**
- **C A scope statement**
- **D A business case**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

One of the inputs to the Develop Project Charter process that describes the necessary information
from a business standpoint to determine whether the expected outcomes of the project justify the
required investment.
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

The business case is the only one of the answer choices that is an input to the Develop Project
Charter process. The business case describes the necessary information from a business
standpoint to determine whether the expected outcomes of the project justify the required
investment.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

- **A The integration plan**
Incorrect. This is a made-up term but refers to what is called the project management plan.
Develop Project Management Plan is the process of defining, preparing, and coordinating
all plan components and consolidating them into an integrated project management plan.
Since the project management plan is created after the project charter, it would not be an
appropriate answer choice.
- **B The project management plan**
Incorrect. The project charter is created before the project management plan, so it would
not be available to you as a reference at this stage in the process.
- **C A scope statement**
Incorrect. The scope statement is created later, as an output of the Define Scope process.
- **D A business case**
Correct. The business case lists the objectives and reasons for project initiation and is one
of the formal inputs to the Develop Project Charter process.

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 6
Question 16 of 200
Question ID: 612749
- **A construction project is almost complete when a stakeholder indicates that the type of tree used**
for landscaping is different from the one specified in the project scope. The project manager tries
to track this change back to its origin but is unable to find any evidence.
What was the most likely reason for this issue?
- **A The tree type was not included in the configuration management plan as a configuration**
item
- **B The stakeholder's comment can be ignored as any type of tree can be used on any**
construction project
- **C The stakeholder register was incomplete and did not include the stakeholder who raised**
the issue
- **D The lessons learned repository did not capture any knowledge from past projects related to**
trees
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

What does the configuration management plan define?
Correct Answer: A

**Explanation:**

The scenario implies the Control Scope is being performed. Several components of the project
management plan are inputs to this process. The configuration management plan is the
component of the project management plan that defines those configuration items or items that
require formal change control, and the process for controlling changes to such items. If the type
of trees used for landscaping were a configuration item, changing the type was supposed to
trigger a change request, which would have gone through the organization's change control

---

process established for the project. The change would have been either approved or rejected (or
deferred, depending on the process defined). The inclusion of a configuration item helps to
ensure that the change is documented, allowing the project manager to follow it up. Therefore, of
the available choices, the most likely cause of the issue was that the type of tree was not a
configurable item.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A The tree type was not included in the configuration management plan as a configuration**
item
Correct. The configuration management plan should specify configuration items. If the tree
type is not among these items, it is reasonable to assume that the tree type was changed
without going through the organization's change control process established for the project.
- **B The stakeholder's comment can be ignored as any type of tree can be used on any**
construction project
Incorrect. This statement is absolute. There is not enough information in the question to
support it. Answer choices that use absolute statements are typically incorrect.
Additionally, ignoring stakeholders is unlikely to be the best course of action.
- **C The stakeholder register was incomplete and did not include the stakeholder who raised**
the issue
Incorrect. A stakeholder register is a project document that includes the identification,
assessment, and classification of project stakeholders. In the scenario, the project manager
is trying to track the change back to its origin. The stakeholder register has nothing to do
with tracking changes on a project nor is it an input to the Control Scope process implied
by the scenario.
- **D The lessons learned repository did not capture any knowledge from past projects related to**
trees
Incorrect. A lessons learned repository is an organization process asset (OPA) that captures
knowledge gained from past projects. Whether or not this OPA included any information
about trees has nothing to do with tracking changes to the current project. Also, the way
this answer choice is worded makes it unclear as to what knowledge exactly about trees
would have helped the project manager, if at all.

**Reference:**


---

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 169, 88, 115-116

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 6
Question 17 of 200
Question ID: 612753
As the project started to produce its first deliverables, the customer expresses their frustration
saying that the project does not accommodate quickly changing requirements that are essential to
meet market demand. The project manager states that these rapid changes are slowing the project
down and wreaking havoc on the schedule.
What has the project manager most likely done wrong?
- **A Allowed too many changes instead of being strict on change**
- **B The project manager did nothing wrong; the project should proceed as planned.**
- **C Selected the wrong development life cycle for the project**
- **D Allowed the project to start when the customer did not know what was needed**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

How does a methodology that accommodates change affect the schedule?
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

An important aspect of project management is tailoring the project management methodology to
the needs of the project. A predictive approach works well for projects where requirements can
be determined upfront. In a project environment where the project requirements are continually
evolving, an adaptive approach is suited better. The benefit of adaptive life cycles, such as agile,
is that this approach welcomes changes throughout the development life cycle and harnesses
change to maximize value for the customer. Had the project manager selected an adaptive
approach for the project, the problems described by the question could have likely been avoided.

---

Therefore, it is reasonable to assume that the project manager selected the wrong development
life cycle.
It is likely that a hybrid project management approach would have worked best for this project.
- **A hybrid approach combines elements of traditional projects with those of agile. For example, if**
the organization wants (for whatever reasons) to manage its projects traditionally, the
organization can decide that most of the project processes will be carried out using the predictive
project management approach, while the change management will follow agile practices to meet
the customer's need of frequently changing requirements. Note, the development approach, e.g.,
hybrid, is typically documented as an additional component of the project management plan.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Allowed too many changes instead of being strict on change**
Incorrect. Allowing the changes in itself is not wrong, as long as the changes are controlled
and not the result of poor planning. In a rapidly changing environment like the one
described by the scenario, the project management methodology needs to provide flexibility
in order to maximize value to the customer.
- **B The project manager did nothing wrong; the project should proceed as planned.**
Incorrect. The current approach has been proven wrong. Proceeding as planned would only
worsen the situation and decrease the chances of the project's success. The project
manager should have selected a different development life cycle.
- **C Selected the wrong development life cycle for the project**
Correct. The approach as described in the question is predictive. However, because of the
need for rapid changes, a development life cycle that is adaptive, like an agile approach,
would be more appropriate.
- **D Allowed the project to start when the customer did not know what was needed**
Incorrect. In a project environment where requirements continually evolve, it is not realistic
to wait until all of the requirements are known before starting project work. Rather, the
project methodology needs to provide the flexibility to meet the needs of the project.

**Reference:**


---

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 19, 88, 176-177
Live FeedbackTM Back to Results

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 6
Question 18 of 200
Question ID: 612718
- **A project manager is in the process of conducting procurements for a large infrastructure**
development project, which involves multiple contractors from various countries.
How might the project manager reduce problems and claims during execution?
- **A Avoid using bidder conferences due to international travel expenses**
- **B Use internationally recognized standard contract forms**
- **C Utilize a preapproved seller list**
- **D Authorize the CCB to handle claims administration**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

The laws regarding the enforcement of contracts likely vary among countries.
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

The question implies that the project manager is performing the Conduct Procurements process.
One of the trends and emerging practices associated with Project Procurement Management is
represented by changing contracting processes. International contracts with multiple contractors
from many countries are inherently riskier than projects using only local contractors. For these
projects, the use of internationally recognized standard contract forms is increasing to reduce
problems and claims during administration. Therefore, of the available answer choices, the
project manager should consider using internationally recognized standard contract forms in this
scenario.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Avoid using bidder conferences due to international travel expenses**
Incorrect. Bidder conferences are meetings with prospective sellers prior to the preparation
of a bid or proposal to ensure all prospective vendors have a clear and common
understanding of the procurement. Contractors may or may not be willing to pay for
international travel to attend a bidder conference. The project manager may consider
virtual options for bidder conferences to avoid international travel but avoiding bidder
conferences would not reduce claims during execution.
- **B Use internationally recognized standard contract forms**
Correct. The use of internationally recognized standard contract forms should be
considered to reduce problems and claims during the administration of a project involving
multiple contractors from various countries.
- **C Utilize a preapproved seller list**
Incorrect. A preapproved seller list is a list of sellers that have been properly vetted, which
can streamline the steps needed to advertise the opportunity and shorten the timeline for
the seller selection process. A preapproved seller list may or may not be used when dealing
with international contractors. However, utilizing a preapproved seller list is not likely to
reduce claims during execution.
- **D Authorize the CCB to handle claims administration**
Incorrect. A change control board (CCB) is a formally chartered group responsible for
reviewing, evaluating, approving, delaying, or rejecting changes to the project. A CCB
would not be involved in claims administration.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 463

PMP Exam 6
Question 19 of 200
Question ID: 612197
- **A project team is testing a prototype of a new drone. Something goes wrong and causes the**
drone to crash and explode. Fortunately, this risk has been identified early in the project, and the
contingency reserves allocated for the risk are sufficient to construct another prototype.
What should the project manager do next?
- **A Submit a change request to update the cost baseline**
- **B Use the contingency reserves to construct a new prototype**
- **C Submit a change request to tap into the contingency reserves**
- **D Terminate the project since the only prototype was destroyed**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

The remaining reserves are adequate to build a new drone.
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

The question describes a situation where a risk has been realized, which would incur a cost to the
project. Realized risks are addressed using the Implement Risk Responses process. A risk
register, an input to this process, would be reviewed to find the response planned for this risk.
Reserve analysis should be conducted to assess if the contingency reserves are adequate to cover
the risk response. According to the scenario, the existing contingency reserves are sufficient to
cover the cost to construct another prototype drone and, therefore, those reserves can be used to
build a new prototype without a need to submit a change request.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Submit a change request to update the cost baseline**
Incorrect. The question states that the contingency reserves are sufficient to cover the cost
of building a new prototype. Contingency reserves are included as part of the cost baseline.
- **B Use the contingency reserves to construct a new prototype**
Correct. The scenario implies that reserve analysis has been done, and it was found that the
contingency reserves are sufficient to build a new drone. Therefore, the next logical step is
to construct the new drone using the contingency reserves.
- **C Submit a change request to tap into the contingency reserves**
Incorrect. Contingency reserves are included in the cost baseline. Since the project
manager has direct control over the funds in the cost baseline, a change request is not
required to tap into the contingency reserves.
- **D Terminate the project since the only prototype was destroyed**
Incorrect. Terminating the project is unlikely based on the information presented.
Contingency reserves are sufficient to cover the cost to construct another prototype drone.

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 450, 456

Question ID: 613658
- **A project manager is creating a schedule and coordinating activities with all of the various**
vendors that have been contracted to perform work on the project.
Where is the best place for the project manager to find any known supplier scheduling
constraints?
- **A Procurement management plan**
- **B Project schedule**
- **C Agreements**
- **D Schedule baseline**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

What collection of documents might contain details of agreed-upon timelines with vendors?
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

The question implies that the Develop Schedule process is underway. One of the inputs to the
Develop Schedule process is agreements. Agreements can take the form of a contract,
memorandum of understanding (MOU), letters of agreement, verbal agreements, email, etc.
Vendor agreements may already exist before the development of the schedule and may include
vendor scheduling constraints. The project manager needs to take into account any vendor
agreements that may affect the timeline when developing the project schedule.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Procurement management plan**
Incorrect. The procurement management plan is a component of the project management
plan that describes how a project team will acquire goods and services from outside of the
performing organization. However, the procurement management plan does not have
details of vendor availability.
- **B Project schedule**
Incorrect. The question suggests that the Develop Schedule process is being carried out.
The project schedule is an output of the Develop Schedule process rather than an input.
- **C Agreements**
Correct. Agreements with vendors may already exist before the development of the project
schedule. It will be necessary for the project manager to understand any agreed-upon
scheduling constraints before developing the schedule.
- **D Schedule baseline**
Incorrect. It can be inferred from the question that the Develop Schedule process is being
performed. The schedule baseline is one of the outputs of the Develop Schedule process and
not an input.

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 6
Question 21 of 200
Question ID: 612759
Executive stakeholders are failing to engage in a project.
What is the best course of action for the project manager?
- **A Do nothing as executives are superior to project managers**
- **B Escalate the issue to the project sponsor**
- **C Work with the executives to improve their engagement**
- **D Update the stakeholder register**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

- **A collaborative approach is usually best.**
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

The scenario covers two project management processes, Manage Stakeholder Engagement, and
Monitor Stakeholder Engagement. The former is focused on communicating and working with
stakeholders to meet their needs and expectations, address issues, and foster appropriate
stakeholder involvement. The latter is concerned with monitoring stakeholder relationships and
tailoring strategies for engaging stakeholders through modification of engagement strategies and
plans. According to the scenario, the executive stakeholders are disengaged. Therefore, the
project manager should work with them to determine what has to be done to improve the level of
their engagement, which, hopefully, would contribute to their support for the project and
eventually increase the chances of project success.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Do nothing as executives are superior to project managers**
Incorrect. According to the scenario, the executives are project stakeholders. Keeping
stakeholders, especially executives, engaged would allow the project manager to increase
their support for the project, thus improving the chances of project success. Doing nothing,
on the other hand, would decrease those chances.
- **B Escalate the issue to the project sponsor**
Incorrect. Escalating the issue to the project sponsor is a premature action. The project
manager should first work directly with the executive stakeholders to identify the issues
causing the lack of engagement and then attempt to address those issues. If all reasonable
efforts fail, and the lack of stakeholder engagement is negatively affecting the project, then
the project manager should seek assistance from the project sponsor.
- **C Work with the executives to improve their engagement**
Correct. The project manager needs to collaborate with the executive stakeholders to
address the gap in the level of their engagement.
- **D Update the stakeholder register**
Incorrect. It is true that the stakeholder register will need to be updated to reflect the
current level of the stakeholder engagement. However, the question is asking about the
'best' (not 'first') course of action. In other words, the question is looking for the answer
choice that represents an action aiming to resolve the problem described in the question,
which is the insufficient level of stakeholder engagement. Simply updating stakeholder
register would not resolve the problem.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 534-535

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 6
Question 22 of 200
Question ID: 612324
The risk management plan for the project stipulates that the project hold risk review meetings
weekly.
Which of the following are you least likely to do during these meetings?
- **A Capture knowledge gained in the lessons learned register**
- **B Create the risk register**
- **C Update the risk report**
- **D Revise the issue log**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Which of the answer choices represents an activity that should be performed as part of the
Identify Risks process rather than the Monitor Risks process?
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

Risk review meetings may be held as part of the Monitor Risks process. Risk reviews are
regularly scheduled and should examine and document the effectiveness of risk responses in
dealing with overall project risk and with identified individual project risks. Risk reviews may
also result in the identification of new individual project risks (including secondary risks that
arise from risks responses), reassessment of current risks, the closing of risks that are outdated,
issues that have arisen as the result of risks that have occurred, and identification of lessons to be
learned for implementation in the current project or future projects.
Keep in mind that the question is asking for the activity that is 'least' likely to be conducted
during a risk review meeting. A risk review meeting is conducted as part of the Monitor Risks

---

process. The risk register may be 'updated' during a risk review meeting, but the risk register is
'created' as an output of the Identify Risks process rather than the Monitor Risks process.
Therefore, of the available choices, creating the risk register is the 'least' likely activity to be
performed during a risk review meeting.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Capture knowledge gained in the lessons learned register**
Incorrect. The lessons learned register is a project document used to record knowledge
gained during a project, so that it can be used in the current project and entered into the
lessons learned repository. Risk reviews may result in the identification of lessons to be
learned for implementation in the current project or future projects.
- **B Create the risk register**
Correct. A risk review meeting is conducted as part of the Monitor Risks process. The risk
register may be 'updated' during a risk review meeting, but the risk register is 'created' as
an output of the Identify Risks process rather than the Monitor Risks process.
- **C Update the risk report**
Incorrect. The risk report is a project document, which summarizes information on
individual project risks and the level of overall project risk. Risk reviews may result in the
identification of new individual project risks and a reassessment of current risks. The risk
report may be updated to include new risks affecting overall project risk, which were
identified during the risk review meeting, or a change to current risks, which were
previously documented in the risk report.
- **D Revise the issue log**
Incorrect. The issue log is a project document, where information about issues is recorded
and monitored. Risk reviews may result in the identification of issues that have arisen as the
result of risks that have occurred. This information should then be recorded in the issue log
where it can be tracked and monitored.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 457
Live FeedbackTM Back to Results

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 6
Question 23 of 200
Question ID: 612816
You have just taken over a project, which is halfway complete. An earned value analysis
indicates that the project is ahead of schedule and under budget. You want to reward your team
and need to see what recognition and rewards have been approved for the project.
What should you do first?
- **A Review the recognition and rewards register**
- **B Check the project management plan**
- **C Ask the project team what recognition and rewards they would prefer**
- **D Call the human resources department for assistance**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

During project planning, a determination is made as to which recognition and rewards will be
given to team members, and when they will be given.
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

Recognition and rewards are an important aspect of the Develop Team process that, according to
the scenario described, you are about to carry out. The recognition plan is an element of the
resource management plan which, in turn, is a component of the project management plan. The
recognition plan should outline what recognition and rewards will be given to team members,
and when they will be given. Therefore, to see what recognition and rewards have been approved
for the project, you should first check the project management plan.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Review the recognition and rewards register**
Incorrect. 'Recognition and rewards register' is a made-up term.
- **B Check the project management plan**
Correct. The recognition plan within the resource management plan should outline which
recognition and rewards will be given to team members, and when they will be given. The
resource management plan is a component of the project management plan.
- **C Ask the project team what recognition and rewards they would prefer**
Incorrect. While seeking input from the project team may be a good idea, a project
manager should first understand what recognition and rewards have been approved for the
project. If multiple options are available, then discussing the alternatives may be
appropriate.
- **D Call the human resources department for assistance**
Incorrect. The human resources department may or may not be familiar with the
recognition plan for the project. However, there is no reason to contact the human
resources department when the information should be readily available in the project
management plan.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 319, 339
Live FeedbackTM Back to Results

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 6
Question 24 of 200
Question ID: 612220
During a risk review meeting, the project manager learns that the lead developer for the project
has been offered a position with a competitor. The project team members have been with the
performing organization for over ten years, so the risk of losing a developer was considered as
low-probability and placed on the watch list of the risk register.
What is the best course of action?
- **A No further action is necessary since the risk has already been placed on the watch list**
- **B Begin searching for a replacement just in case the developer leaves the company**
- **C Upgrade the risk in the risk register and develop an appropriate risk response plan**
- **D Implement the agreed-upon risk response from the risk register**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Risks recorded on the watch list do not typically have risk responses.
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

Risks that have a low probability and/or impact may be placed on a watch list for future
monitoring. The risk register may include symptoms and warning signs of risk. The fact that a
developer has been offered a position with a competitor is an example of a warning sign and
indicates that the risk of losing a developer has just increased significantly. This situation will
likely warrant removing the risk from the watch list and placing it alongside the other identified
risks in the risk register followed by having a risk response developed and agreed upon in case
the risk is realized. Therefore, of the available options, the best course of action is to upgrade the
risk in the risk register and develop an appropriate risk response plan.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

- **A No further action is necessary since the risk has already been placed on the watch list**
Incorrect. The question describes a situation where a low probability risk was placed on the
watch list, but the probability of that risk occurring has just increased significantly. This
risk should be analyzed and likely upgraded from the watch list to an identified risk with an
appropriately developed risk response plan.
- **B Begin searching for a replacement just in case the developer leaves the company**
Incorrect. With the risk of losing a developer placed on the watch list, it is unlikely that a
response plan has been developed for this risk. As such, a risk response plan should be
developed and agreed upon first. The risk response plan may or may not involve searching
for a suitable replacement. Regardless, the risk should be analyzed before action is taken to
address the risk.
- **C Upgrade the risk in the risk register and develop an appropriate risk response plan**
Correct. With the risk of losing a developer placed on the watch list, it is unlikely that a
response plan has been developed to address this risk. The risk should be removed from the
watch list and upgraded, at which point a risk response should be developed to address the
risk.
- **D Implement the agreed-upon risk response from the risk register**
Incorrect. Since the risk was placed on the watch list, it is unlikely that a risk response has
been developed. Additionally, the risk of losing a developer has increased but has yet to be
realized. Therefore, implementing the agreed-upon risk response, even if one was
developed, is a premature action.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 455, 458
Live FeedbackTM Back to Results

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 6
Question 25 of 200
Question ID: 612635
You have just started a project. Some of the risks that you are anticipating for this project might
have surfaced in previous projects.
Which of the following would you review to see how these risks and issues were handled?
- **A Policies and procedures**
- **B Project closure documents from previous documents**
- **C Lessons learned repository**
- **D Lesson learned register**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

All of the answer choices represent types of organizational process assets, but which contains
risk information from previous projects?
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

The scenario implies you are in the Plan Risk Management process. Information on risks from
previous projects is recorded in the lessons learned repository, an organizational process asset,
which is an input to the Plan Risk Management process. Lessons learned repository is used to
learn about risks identified in previous projects to determine whether similar risks might recur
during the current project and to learn about how they were handled. Note that the lessons
learned ‘register’ might seem like a good pick, however, the register tracks risks for the current
project. Therefore, of the available choices, reviewing the lessons learned repository is the best
answer to the question asked.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Policies and procedures**
Incorrect. Policies and procedures are organizational process assets which set guidelines,
standards, and criteria for an organization. However, policies and procedures do not
include historical information on risks.
- **B Project closure documents from previous documents**
Incorrect. Project closure documents consist of formal documentation that indicates
completion of the project and the transfer of the completed project deliverables to others,
such as an operations group. Even though project closure documents are considered
historical information, they do not contain information on past risks.
- **C Lessons learned repository**
Correct. The lessons learned repository is a store of historical information about lessons
learned from projects. The lessons learned repository may provide information on risks
from previous projects. This information can be used to identify if risks that you are
anticipating for this project occurred on previous projects, and what risk responses worked
well to handle them.
- **D Lesson learned register**
Incorrect. The lessons learned register is a project document that is used to record
knowledge gained during the current project. Since you are looking for information about
risks encountered during previous projects, reviewing the lessons learned register is
unlikely to help you.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 403
