PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 6
Top of Form
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 102 of 200
Question ID: 650804
- **A project manager is in the process of developing cost estimates. Many risks have been**
identified on this project, and the project manager understands that cost estimates should account
for the contingency reserves associated with these risks.
What should the project manager do as part of this process to account for the cost of uncertainty?
Top of Form
- **A Perform reserve analysis**
- **B Conduct a risk audit**
- **C Develop the risk management plan**
- **D Calculate the cost of quality**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

What component of the cost baseline addresses identified risks?
Correct Answer: A

**Explanation:**

This question involves two project management Knowledge Areas - Risk Management and Cost
Management. The scenario suggests that the project manager is conducting the Estimate Costs
process. Reserve analysis is an example of a data analysis technique that can be used in this
process. Cost estimates may include contingency reserves to account for cost uncertainty.
Contingency reserves are the budget within the cost baseline that is allocated for identified risks.

---

Contingency reserves are often viewed as part of the budget intended to address the
known-unknowns that can affect a project. Hence, the project manager should first perform a
reserve analysis to determine the amount of contingency reserves needed to develop the cost
estimates.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Perform reserve analysis**
Correct. Contingency reserves are established to cover identified risks. Reserve analysis is
used to estimate the amount of budget required to account for these risks. Reserve analysis
is an example of the data analysis technique that can be used as part of the Estimate Costs
process implied by the scenario.
- **B Conduct a risk audit**
Incorrect. A risk audit is a technique used to consider the effectiveness of the risk
management process. A risk audit is typically conducted as part of the processes of the
Monitoring and Controlling Process Group, while according to the scenario the project is
still in planning.
- **C Develop the risk management plan**
Incorrect. The risk management plan is an output of the Plan Risk Management process.
According to the scenario, the risks have already been identified. The Plan Risk
Management process is typically performed earlier in the project life cycle, implying the
risk management plan has already been developed.
- **D Calculate the cost of quality**
Incorrect. The cost of quality includes all costs incurred over the life of the product by
investment in preventing nonconformance to requirements, appraisal of the product or
service for conformance to requirements, and failure to meet requirements. The question is
asking about accounting for costs associated with identified project risks rather than the
cost of quality.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 245

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 6
Top of Form
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 103 of 200
Question ID: 612320
- **A project produces pistons and connecting rods with extremely tight tolerances. The first few**
pistons were scrapped, as they were not within the limits specified by the contract. The identified
risk response was the acquisition of equipment that could machine pistons more precisely.
With the new equipment in place, what should be done next to determine the effectiveness of the
risk response?
Top of Form
- **A Make a test run to gather work performance information**
- **B Perform technical performance analysis**
- **C Produce a test batch to gather work performance data**
- **D Produce all of the pistons required by the contract and then scrap any that fall outside the**
specification limits
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

You, as the project manager, need first to collect raw data to determine the effectiveness of the
risk response.
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

During project execution, work performance data may be produced which can then be analyzed
as part of the Monitoring and Controlling Process Group to produce work performance

---

information. Work performance data serves as an input to various monitoring and controlling
processes including the Monitor Risks process. In this case, a batch of pistons must first be
produced using the new equipment, and then measurements must be taken. This raw data
represents work performance data. The work performance data can then be analyzed to
determine if the new equipment can produce pistons with the required precision. In this manner,
the effectiveness of the risk response can be determined. Therefore, of the choices offered,
producing a test batch to gather work performance data is what you, as the project manager,
should do next to determine the effectiveness of the risk response.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Make a test run to gather work performance information**
Incorrect. Work performance data, once analyzed, becomes work performance information.
Work performance data must first be collected before it can be analyzed to produce the
work performance information.
- **B Perform technical performance analysis**
Incorrect. Technical performance analysis is a data analysis technique that may be
performed in order to determine the effectiveness of a risk response. Before any analysis
can be performed, at least some pistons must be produced with the new equipment and then
measurements taken to determine if they meet the specifications.
- **C Produce a test batch to gather work performance data**
Correct. A batch of pistons must first be produced, and then measurements must be taken.
These measurements represent work performance data. The work performance data can
then be analyzed to determine if the new equipment can produce pistons with the required
precision. In this manner, the effectiveness of the risk response can be determined.
- **D Produce all of the pistons required by the contract and then scrap any that fall outside the**
specification limits
Incorrect. Producing all of the pistons required by the contract introduces needless risk. If
all of the pistons produced fall outside the required specifications, the entire production run
must be scrapped. It is better to produce a small batch of pistons first to determine if the
new equipment can produce pistons with the required precision, or if further action is
required to meet the contractual obligations.

**Reference:**


---

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 456
Bottom of Form

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 6
Top of Form
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 104 of 200
Question ID: 612844
You have recently taken over a project from someone who is on leave. You have concerns about
scope creep on the project. You want to understand if there are any variances in scope and if the
variance is within the threshold amount or if corrective or preventive action is appropriate.
With which of the following should you compare the actual results to make this determination?
Top of Form
- **A Requirements documentation**
- **B Work performance data**
- **C Requirements traceability matrix**
- **D Scope baseline**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

During the Control Scope process, you are reviewing actual versus planned results in terms of
scope, so think about which information source contains the planned results.
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

In order to control scope, the project manager uses the scope baseline to find variances to scope,
which may represent scope creep. The scope baseline is the approved version of the scope
statement, work breakdown structure (WBS), and its associated WBS dictionary, that can be
changed using formal change control procedures and is used as a basis for comparison to actual

---

results. The scope baseline represents the planned scope of the project. During the Control Scope
process, the scope baseline is compared to actual results to determine if a change, corrective
action, or preventive action is necessary. The incorrect answer choices are also inputs to the
Control Scope process, but they are not the primary document used to determine if a variance in
the project scope has occurred. Therefore, of the available options, the scope baseline is the best
answer to the question asked.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Requirements documentation**
Incorrect. The requirements documentation provides a description of how individual
requirements meet the business need for the project. Although the requirements
documentation may have some beneficial information concerning scope creep, it is not the
approved version of the project scope.
- **B Work performance data**
Incorrect. Work performance data is the raw observations and measurements identified
during activities being performed to carry out the project work. Work performance data
represents the actual results which you have already obtained. The question is asking to
compare the actual results with something that will help understand if there is any scope
creep on the project. Comparing the actual results with the actual results (represented by
the work performance data) makes no sense.
- **C Requirements traceability matrix**
Incorrect. The requirements traceability matrix is a grid that links product requirements
from their origin to the deliverables that satisfy them. This matrix would provide some
information to investigate any deviations from the scope, but it would not be easy to find
variances in scope by simply using the matrix.
- **D Scope baseline**
Correct. Baselines are used as a basis for comparison to actual results and can help
determine variances. In this case, the scope baseline can be used to find any variances in
scope.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 170
Bottom of Form

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 6
Top of Form
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 105 of 200
Question ID: 613150
- **A project has recently started the design phase and there are multiple change requests per week**
altering the requirements. The project manager feels there is a bigger issue to address.
Which of the following would be the least logical approach in this situation?
Top of Form
- **A Collect and analyze the change request data**
- **B Suggest switching the project to an agile methodology**
- **C Increase the length and cost of the project to accommodate the changes**
- **D Raise a risk that if the changes continue at the current rate, the project is at risk of failing**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Projects need to accommodate change.
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

The question depicts a project that has numerous and frequent change requests, which then result
in ever altering requirements. It is an issue that falls under the Control Scope process. The
question alludes to a "bigger issue" but does not define what that problem might be. It would be
reasonable to collect and analyze the change request data to gain a better understanding of what
is driving the excessive change requests. Additionally, it would be a good idea to notify the
stakeholders of the impact of all the requested changes. However, requesting a revision to the

---

baselines is not a reasonable action until the "bigger issue" is clearly understood. It is likely that
the issues driving the excessive change requests can be addressed without revising the baselines.
Therefore, increasing the length and cost of the project to accommodate the changes is a
premature action at this point and the 'least' logical approach to addressing the problem described
in this scenario.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Collect and analyze the change request data**
Incorrect. The question alludes to a "bigger issue" but does not define what that problem
might be. It would be reasonable to collect and analyze the change request data and then
take action to understand better the requirements, which may, in turn, reduce the volume of
change requests.
- **B Suggest switching the project to an agile methodology**
Incorrect. This choice describes a logical approach since agile can accommodate high
rates of change in a project, and this project may benefit from an adaptive methodology like
agile.
- **C Increase the length and cost of the project to accommodate the changes**
Correct. This answer choice represents a premature action. There is not yet enough
information to create a change request to update the cost and schedule baselines. The
project manager should first analyze the situation to understand why there are so many
change requests. It is likely that these issues can be addressed and avoid changing the
baselines.
- **D Raise a risk that if the changes continue at the current rate, the project is at risk of failing**
Incorrect. This choice describes a logical reaction to ensure that stakeholders are aware
that the rate of changes might jeopardize the successful completion of the project.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 169

Question 106 of 200
Question ID: 613412
You are leading a project to build a production line for the engine parts in a new electric vehicle.
The inspection of the parts created by the initial run of the line has resulted in an unacceptably
high failure rate. However, an audit conducted by an independent quality team reports that it is
the inspection routine that was flawed and that almost all of the questionable parts do in fact
meet the specifications.
What is your next step?
Top of Form
- **A Meet with the production line design team to determine what changes need to be made to the**
line
- **B Update the quality management plan to remove the flawed inspection routine**
- **C Meet with the quality team to determine what changes are required in the quality management**
plan
- **D Update the scope, schedule and cost baselines to incorporate an improved inspection routine**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Before taking any action, you should understand what the problem is.
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**


---

The scenario implies you are carrying out the Manage Quality process. The problem identified
by the audit is not the production line, but the inspection routine. Therefore, changes will be
needed in the quality management plan. Before you can initiate changes, you first need to
determine what those changes should be, and the team will be the best resource to accomplish
this. Then you can use the Perform Integrated Change Control process to update the appropriate
plans and documents.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Meet with the production line design team to determine what changes need to be made to**
the line
Incorrect. According to the audit, the problem lays with the inspection routine, not the
design of the production line.
- **B Update the quality management plan to remove the flawed inspection routine**
Incorrect. Although the quality management plan will need to be updated, you should
improve the flawed inspection routine rather than remove it.
- **C Meet with the quality team to determine what changes are required in the quality**
management plan
Correct. Updates to the quality management plan are an output of the Manage Quality
process and should occur when the agreed-upon approach to managing quality needs to
change due to actual results. The quality team will be the best resource for determining
what changes are needed.
- **D Update the scope, schedule and cost baselines to incorporate an improved inspection**
routine
Incorrect. While changes to the various baselines may eventually be needed, you should
first meet with the quality team to determine what those changes will be.

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page 297

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 6
Top of Form
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 107 of 200
Question ID: 613687
You are in the process of collecting detailed requirements for a user interface (UI) redesign
project. Your stakeholders include business subject matter experts (SMEs) as well as the
software development team. Both groups have vastly different ideas on product requirements,
and the interactions between the groups become tense. You want to build trust, foster
relationships, and achieve stakeholder consensus during requirements collection.
Which method would be best in this situation?
Top of Form
- **A Decision tree analysis**
- **B Facilitation**
- **C Multicriteria decision analysis**
- **D Mind mapping**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

What interpersonal skill, used to collect requirements, can guide a diverse group to a favorable
decision, solution, or conclusion?
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

In this scenario, you have two groups of stakeholders who have a difference of opinion on the
requirements of the redesigned UI, and yet you need to elicit requirements from them both.

---

Facilitation is a technique that can be used in cross-functional workshops to define requirements
and reconcile stakeholder differences. Well facilitated sessions can build trust, foster
relationships, and improve communication among participants, which can lead to increased
stakeholder consensus. While some of the answer choices provided are tools and techniques that
can be used during the Collect Requirements process described in the question, under the
circumstances presented, facilitation would be the best technique as it can assist with collecting
requirements as well as build relationship among the stakeholders who have vastly different
ideas on the product requirements.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Decision tree analysis**
Incorrect. The decision tree analysis is used to support the selection of several alternative
courses of action. This data analysis technique is used when performing quantitative data
analysis (typically for the Perform Quantitative Risk Analysis process). In this situation, the
stakeholders are not trying to analyze quantitative data. Facilitation would be more
appropriate to achieve consensus among stakeholders.
- **B Facilitation**
Correct. Facilitation is a technique that can be used in cross-functional workshops to
define requirements. Well facilitated sessions can build trust, foster relationships, and
improve communication among participants, which can lead to increased stakeholder
consensus. Under the circumstances described in the scenario, facilitation is the best
technique to use.
- **C Multicriteria decision analysis**
Incorrect. Multicriteria decision analysis uses a systematic approach to evaluate and rank
many ideas. While multicriteria decision analysis is a technique that can be applied during
the Collect Requirements process, this technique is less helpful in the scenario described
where stakeholders have vastly different ideas on the product requirements. In this
situation, to achieve consensus among stakeholders, facilitation will likely be a more
effective tool for the project manager to use.
- **D Mind mapping**
Incorrect. Mind mapping is a data representation technique used on data created through
brainstorming sessions. Although mind mapping is one of the tools and techniques used
during the Collect Requirement process, it is not the best tool to use to achieve consensus
among the stakeholders.

---


**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 145, 80
Bottom of Form

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 6
Top of Form
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 108 of 200
Question ID: 650603
- **A project is running a month ahead of schedule partly because many of the identified project**
risks did not occur. The project is expected to finish within budget but does not have the money
to pay vendor invoices upon its early completion. The project manager informs the vendors that
their invoices will be paid later, on the originally planned project completion date.
What is the most likely reason?
Top of Form
- **A Risk register did not account for the positive risk**
- **B Cost estimates were too low**
- **C The project schedule had too much buffer**
- **D Funding requirements**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

How is capital typically allocated to a project?
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

There is no indication that the project has overspent. In fact, the question states that the project is
expected to finish within budget. The only other way the project could be low on capital is to
have not gotten funding. Funding is typically allocated to a project in increments rather than the
entire budget being made available at the start of the project. It is most likely that the funding

---

requirements were not adjusted to account for needing the funds to be released earlier. Therefore,
of the available choices, funding requirements is the most likely reason for the project to be
unable to pay vendor invoices.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Risk register did not account for the positive risk**
Incorrect. There is no indication that there was an opportunity that was exploited, just that
negative risks were avoided.
- **B Cost estimates were too low**
Incorrect. The question states that the project is expected to finish within budget. Hence,
the cost estimates are not the problem in this scenario.
- **C The project schedule had too much buffer**
Incorrect. There are likely unused schedule reserves for the risks that were not encountered.
Encountering fewer or less severe risk events probably accounts for the project being ahead
of schedule. However, avoiding project risks should not make the project fall short of cash.
- **D Funding requirements**
Correct. Since the project does not seem to have overspent the budget but does not have the
cash to pay invoices, it is most likely that the funding requirements were not adjusted to
account for needing the funds to be released sooner.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 256

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 6
Top of Form
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 109 of 200
Question ID: 610090
While performing project work, a team member notices that there is a potential new risk, which
could impact the project's critical path.
What should the team member do immediately?
Top of Form
- **A Recommend the project be placed on hold for a day to avoid the risk**
- **B Document the risk in the risk register**
- **C Draft an emergency fallback plan since the critical path is in jeopardy**
- **D Generate a risk report using quantitative and quantitative analysis of the identified risk to alert**
the team of the schedule impacts
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

The team member needs to act quickly so that this risk is not forgotten.
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

By recording identified risks in the risk register, the project manager and team are able to keep
track of all potential threats and opportunities. Furthermore, once a risk has been analyzed using
qualitative and or quantitative risk analysis methods, the risk register serves as the central

---

repository for planned risk responses and lists risk owners. As such, any time a new risk emerges
on a project, the first step to take is to immediately document it in the risk register.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Recommend the project be placed on hold for a day to avoid the risk**
Incorrect. If this risk was previously identified and its planned risk response was to place
the project on hold for a day, then if the risk occurred, applying its planned response would
have been the right thing to do. However, based on the scenario described, this risk is new.
Therefore, the immediate step to take for any newly identified risk is to document it in the
risk register rather than applying an action that has not been defined as the appropriate
response to that risk.
- **B Document the risk in the risk register**
Correct. The risk register acts as a repository in which identified risks are recorded,
including the outputs of other risk management processes. The immediate first step for the
team member to take is to document the new risk in the risk register so that it will not be
forgotten. The team member should then consult the project risk management plan for
information about what to do next.
- **C Draft an emergency fallback plan since the critical path is in jeopardy**
Incorrect. A fallback plan is a plan that includes an alternative set of actions and tasks
available in the event that the primary plan needs to be abandoned because of subsequent
issues, or an initial risk response does not deal with a risk as effectively as desired. Since
the risk identified by the team member is a new risk, it should first be documented in the
risk register, analyzed, and a risk response and a fallback plan should be developed
(alternatively, a fallback plan can be developed after the risk is realized and the planned
risk response fails).
- **D Generate a risk report using quantitative and quantitative analysis of the identified risk to**
alert the team of the schedule impacts
Incorrect. A risk report is a document that is developed progressively throughout the
project risk management processes which summarizes information on individual project
risks and the level of overall project risk. As an immediate first step, it would not be
appropriate for the team member to generate a risk report since the risk has only just now
been discovered. Once the risk has been added to the risk register, the team member may
then generate a risk report which describes any threats and/or opportunities, risk

---

distribution by category, and which sources of risk create the most risk exposure for the
project.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 417
Bottom of Form

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 6
Top of Form
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 110 of 200
Question ID: 612828
As you prepare to gather requirements for a project you are leading, a review of the lessons
learned repository suggests that improvements need to be made in the software development
process.
What is your best course of action?
Top of Form
- **A Invite the development team to a project retrospective**
- **B Schedule a JAD session with the development team and subject matter experts**
- **C Review and update the requirements management plan as needed**
- **D Analyze the project business documents and modify as required**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

How might facilitation skills be used in the Collect Requirements process to improve the
software development process?
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

The question suggests that the Collect Requirements process is being performed. Joint
application design/development (JAD) sessions are used in the software development industry.
These facilitated sessions focus on bringing business subject matter experts and the development
team together to gather requirements and improve the software development process. To

---

efficiently conduct the JAD sessions, the project manager should use their interpersonal and team
skills such as facilitation which is among the tools and techniques of the Collect Requirements
process. The incorrect answer choices represent actions that cannot be completed based on the
sole authority of the project manager or would not affect the performance of the current project.
Therefore, of the available options, scheduling a JAD session with the development team and
subject matter experts is the best course of action.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Invite the development team to a project retrospective**
Incorrect. A project retrospective is a scheduled review to document lessons learned held at
the end of a project and would not help the Collect Requirement process described in the
scenario which happens much earlier in the project life cycle.
- **B Schedule a JAD session with the development team and subject matter experts**
Correct. Joint application design/development (JAD) sessions focus on bringing business
subject matter experts and the development team together to gather requirements and
improve the software development process.
- **C Review and update the requirements management plan as needed**
Incorrect. The requirements management plan specifies how requirements will be analyzed,
documented, and managed. It does not describe the software development process used on
the project.
- **D Analyze the project business documents and modify as required**
Incorrect. The project business documents include the business case and benefits
management plan, which are created as part of pre-project work. The business documents
are maintained by the project sponsor and cannot be modified by a project manager
without authorization. Additionally, those documents are not concerned with the software
development process.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 145

Question 111 of 200
Question ID: 613049
- **A project to build a new bridge is nearly complete. A city council member tells the painting**
contractor to paint the bridge green instead of blue, but the vendor continues painting the bridge
blue. The council member confronts the project manager and demands that the painting stop or
payment will not be authorized. The project manager checks the change log and then with the
CCB, but no information is available.
What is the project manager's most likely next step?
Top of Form
- **A Instruct the painting contractor to change the color**
- **B Escalate the issue to the executive sponsor**
- **C Use the change management plan to educate the city council member on the correct process**
- **D Determine the cost of the change and ask the city council member to approve the change in cost.**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

What is required to change a project deliverable?
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

The question implies that the city council member went directly to the vendor to implement a
change to the project's deliverable, rather than following the established change control process.
The project manager needs to start by explaining the change request process to the city council

---

member to avoid the issue from recurring. If the city council member still wants the color
changed, then a change request needs to be submitted to the change control board (CCB) along
with any supporting information including estimates for cost and time. Additionally, since it is
reasonable to assume that the work is being completed as contracted, the city council member
would not have legal grounds to withhold payment.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Instruct the painting contractor to change the color**
Incorrect. A change to a project deliverable requires an approved change request prior to
implementation. Since the requested change has not been submitted and approved, it should
not be implemented at this point.
- **B Escalate the issue to the executive sponsor**
Incorrect. The problem described in the question is one that the project manager should be
able to handle and should not require escalation at this point.
- **C Use the change management plan to educate the city council member on the correct**
process
Correct. The question implies that the change was not submitted for approval. As any
change to a project deliverable requires an approved change request, the project manager
needs to start by explaining the change process.
- **D Determine the cost of the change and ask the city council member to approve the change**
in cost.
Incorrect. An estimate of the cost to change the color may be necessary, and the city
council member may need to approve any incremental cost. However, the question mentions
the existence of a change control board (CCB). As such, the CCB will be responsible for
approving any change requests and not just the city council member. In this case, a change
request must be submitted and approved before the change can be implemented.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 169
Bottom of Form

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 6

Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 112 of 200
Question ID: 612750
On a construction project, the project manager finds that the framers are showing up too soon
after the concrete foundation is poured. After a quick look, the project manager figures out that
the curing time was accidentally left out of the schedule.
What part of the schedule model has a problem?
Top of Form
- **A Scheduling register**
- **B Scheduling maintenance**
- **C Market conditions**
- **D Project information**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

- **A schedule model consists of three components.**
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

The project management team selects a scheduling method, such as the critical path method or an
agile approach. Then the project-specific data, such as the activities, planned dates, durations,
resources, dependencies, and constraints, are entered into a scheduling tool to create a schedule
model for the project. The scheduling model consists of three components including the
scheduling method, the scheduling tool, and project information. The project information

---

includes leads and lags as components. Lag time is the amount of time a successor activity will
be delayed with respect to a predecessor activity, such as the time associated with waiting for the
concrete to cure before framing can begin. Hence, the question implies that the lag time
associated with the curing of the concrete was overlooked and not entered into the scheduling
tool. Lag time is a component of the project information, which is an element of the schedule
model. Therefore, among the available choices, project information is the best answer to the
question asked.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Scheduling register**
Incorrect. 'Scheduling register' is a made-up term.
- **B Scheduling maintenance**
Incorrect. While it is true that once a schedule model is developed that it needs to be
maintained, schedule maintenance is not a component of a schedule model. The question is
asking for one of the three components of a schedule model.
- **C Market conditions**
Incorrect. Market conditions are considered enterprise environmental factors that can
influence several project management processes. However, market conditions are not part
of the project schedule or the schedule model and, therefore, unlikely to be the reason for
the problem described in the scenario.
- **D Project information**
Correct. The question suggests that the lag time associated with the curing of the concrete
was overlooked. Lag time is a component of the project information, which is entered into
the scheduling tool to create the schedule model.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 175-176, 192-193

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 6
Top of Form
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 113 of 200
Question ID: 613295
- **A company has been awarded a contract to build a new bridge across a river connecting two**
states. Funding for the bridge comes from both the state and federal governments. The project
manager plans to use social media to communicate with the public.
What should the project manager do first?
Top of Form
- **A Create a social media policy from scratch**
- **B Check the resource management plan for social media guidelines**
- **C Do not use social media because the conversation cannot be controlled and too many people can**
post negative comments about the project
- **D Get the state and federal communication guidelines and reconcile them with the company's social**
media policy
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

There are likely to be several different policies and guidelines that need to be considered.
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

Since the project will be using state and federal funds, there are likely to be guidelines
established by these governments that apply to any vendors. Additionally, it is likely that the
performing organization has their own social media policy. The project manager should reconcile

---

all of the applicable policies and guidelines in the development of the project's social media
communication strategy. This action will help ensure compliance with all communication
requirements regarding the use of social media.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Create a social media policy from scratch**
Incorrect. The performing organization likely already has a corporate social media policy.
If a policy does not exist, then the project manager may need to create guidelines for the
use of social media. In this case, there are three main funding sources for this project. It is
safe to assume that each government entity has communication guidelines that should be
followed when using public funding, and these guidelines can form the basis for the
project's social media communication strategy. Therefore, there is no reason to create a
social media policy from scratch.
- **B Check the resource management plan for social media guidelines**
Incorrect. As it pertains to project communications, the resource management plan
describes the communications that are needed for management of the team or physical
resources. The resource management plan is not likely to have any relevant information
regarding using social media to communicate with the public.
- **C Do not use social media because the conversation cannot be controlled and too many**
people can post negative comments about the project
Incorrect. Social media is a way of life and can be an important tool in communicating with
the public. People may attack the project using social media whether the project uses social
media or not. Since the project manager plans to use social media in this scenario,
guidelines for the use of social media on the project should be developed.
- **D Get the state and federal communication guidelines and reconcile them with the**
company's social media policy
Correct. The project manager should reconcile all applicable policies and guidelines in the
development of the project's social media communication strategy.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 383

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 6
Top of Form
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 114 of 200
Question ID: 612761
- **A project manager is tracking the detailed costs of a project in a spreadsheet by listing out each**
task, associated resources (human and other), the resources rates, and the hours the resource is
used. The project is tracking wonderfully. However, after about two months of running the
project, the finance manager approaches the project manager to say the actual project’s costs are
much higher than the project manager is reporting.
What did the project manager most likely do wrong?
Top of Form
- **A Forgot to account for the variable costs of the project resources**
- **B Failed to include indirect costs into the cost baseline**
- **C Nothing is wrong. Higher than planned costs are normal for any project.**
- **D Did not invite the finance manager to the project kick-off meeting**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

The list the project manager is maintaining contains only one type of cost.
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

The question suggests that the project manager has accounted for direct costs but does not
mention anything about indirect costs. By only looking at costs by resource, the project manager
is not taking into consideration costs for overhead items such as meeting rooms, accounting,

---

legal teams, utilities, etc. If the finance manager is charging these indirect costs to the project,
and the project manager has not accounted for these costs, then there will be a discrepancy
between the actual project costs and the costs reported by the project manager. Therefore, in this
situation, the project manager most likely forgot about the indirect costs.
The question does not provide specific details as to how much the actual costs are higher than the
planned costs (the cost baseline). There could be many reasons for the actual costs to be higher
than the planned costs. Whatever the reason is, not including the indirect costs into the cost
baseline makes the variance between the actual costs and planned costs bigger. Therefore, the
most likely reason for the actual costs to be higher than the planned costs in this particular
scenario with the given set of the answer choices is the indirect costs not being included in the
cost baseline.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Forgot to account for the variable costs of the project resources**
Incorrect. The question indicates that the project manager has accounted for the resources
used on the project including the resource rates and hours. These costs are examples of
variable costs. Therefore, the project manager has not just accounted for the fixed costs
associated with the project.
- **B Failed to include indirect costs into the cost baseline**
Correct. By only looking at costs by resource, the project manager is looking only at the
direct costs of the project. Indirect costs need to be added as overhead.
- **C Nothing is wrong. Higher than planned costs are normal for any project.**
Incorrect. Higher than planned costs is not uncommon. However, having higher than
planned costs is not considered normal. Costs must be monitored and controlled, and
variances analyzed and addressed.
- **D Did not invite the finance manager to the project kick-off meeting**
Incorrect. The purpose of the project kick-off meeting is to communicate the objectives of
the project, gain the commitment of the team for the project, and explain the roles and
responsibilities of each stakeholder. The fact the finance manager was (or was not) invited
to the meeting has little to do with the actual costs being higher than planned.

**Reference:**


---

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 246
Bottom of Form
Live FeedbackTM Back to Results

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 6
Top of Form
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 115 of 200
Question ID: 612151
- **A construction company initiates a project to build a shelter in a highly-populated region that has**
been recently destroyed by a natural disaster.
Which of the following represents the fundamental category of factors that led to the initiation of
the project?
Top of Form
- **A Market demand**
- **B New technology**
- **C Social need**
- **D Legal requirement**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

What need is to be satisfied by building the shelter?
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

Building shelter in a region that has been recently destroyed by a natural disaster is an example
of a project initiated to address a social need. Other examples include but are not limited to
providing potable water systems, latrines, and sanitation education to communities suffering
from high rates of infectious diseases. Note, the scenario describes a construction company, not a

---

governmental organization. The fact of being a nongovernmental entity is important for the
project to meet the definition of an initiative that addresses a social need.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Market demand**
Incorrect. Building a very long-lasting smartphone battery to satisfy the needs of the users
is an example of a project to meet market demand. In the scenario, the region has suffered
from a natural disaster, leaving the population without shelter. A shelter is considered a
basic human being need rather than a market demand.
- **B New technology**
Incorrect. A company authorizes a project to build a new rocket which will be able to travel
at speeds close to the speed of light based on the advances in fuel and materials
technologies. Building a shelter for population suffered from a natural disaster is typically
not based on new technologies.
- **C Social need**
Correct. Of the choices provided, building a shelter in a region that has been destroyed by
a natural disaster is best described by addressing a social need.
- **D Legal requirement**
Incorrect. Nothing in the scenario suggests that building a shelter in a region that has been
destroyed by a natural disaster would satisfy a legal requirement.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 9

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 6
Top of Form
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 116 of 200
Question ID: 612578
Execution has begun for a project to establish retail distribution in a new area of the country.
However, the performing organization has just announced the acquisition of a competitor that has
a well-established retail distribution network in the target area rendering the project objectives
obsolete.
What is the best course of action for the performing organization?
Top of Form
- **A Continue with the project as originally planned**
- **B Submit a change request to update the project management plan**
- **C Immediately stop all project work and release the project team**
- **D Terminate the project**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

The need for the project no longer exists.
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

The question implies that the project objectives have been rendered obsolete with the acquisition
of a competitor; thus, the need for the project no longer exists. A project typically ends when its
objectives have been achieved or it is terminated when it cannot or will not meet its objectives,
or when the need for the project no longer exists. The question asks what is the best course of

---

action for the performing organization. The answer is to terminate the project. Note, a project
manager is the person who is authorized by the performing organization to lead the project team
to achieve the project objectives, but the project manager does not have the authority to terminate
a project. An approval from the appropriate authority should be obtained. However, this option is
not provided among the answer choices. Therefore, among the options available, terminating the
project is the best answer to the question asked.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Continue with the project as originally planned**
Incorrect. The question implies that the need for the project no longer exists. Therefore,
there is no reason to continue with the project as originally planned.
- **B Submit a change request to update the project management plan**
Incorrect. The question describes a situation where the need for the project no longer exists
as the result of the acquisition of a competitor. There are no changes that can be made to
the project management plan that can reestablish the value of the project to the performing
organization. Even if the performing organization decides that the acquired retail
distribution network needs to be optimized, this should trigger a new project rather than
altering the project which has been rendered obsolete.
- **C Immediately stop all project work and release the project team**
Incorrect. Although the need for the project no longer exists, there is still project work
which must be completed and finalized, such as the activities of the Close Project or Phase
process. Some of the project team members may still be required to perform these activities.
- **D Terminate the project**
Correct. The question suggests that the need for the project no longer exists. A project's end
is reached when the objectives have been achieved or when the project is terminated
because its objectives will not or cannot be met, or when the need for the project no longer
exists.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 5, 542
Bottom of Form

Question 117 of 200
Question ID: 651333
Executives in a certain business unit of the company have failed to attend project related
meetings. The project manager has sent multiple invites and requests to respond. Another project
manager tells him that he must work with the administrator of the respective business units to get
any response and attendance.
Which skill did the other project manager demonstrate?
Top of Form
- **A Active listening**
- **B Political awareness**
- **C Meeting management**
- **D Social engineering**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

How is one project manager assisting the other project manager?
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

Managing the project communications includes the meetings and interactions with other
managers and executives. If the communications are not reaching their intended audiences or
meeting their intent, then utilizing other tools and techniques to assist the communications may
be necessary. In this scenario, being aware of the power structure, which in this case a gatekeeper

---

in the form of the administrator of the business unit, was important to ensure the communications
were executed as per plans. The other project manager shared his or her political awareness to
assist the project manager to better manage communications.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Active listening**
Incorrect. The project manager was informing another project manager on what course of
action to take. The skill of active listening was not explicitly demonstrated in this scenario.
- **B Political awareness**
Correct. Awareness of the relationships and power structures within the organization is a
skill that the project manager demonstrated by explaining the means to reach and influence
others in a system.
- **C Meeting management**
Incorrect. Meeting management is the skill set used to ensure that meetings run effectively
and efficiently. This skill was not directly and explicitly demonstrated in this scenario.
- **D Social engineering**
Incorrect. Social engineering is the psychological manipulation of people to gain
information or confidential data. Nothing manipulative was done to a person in this
scenario.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 386

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 6
Top of Form
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 118 of 200
Question ID: 612967
Your project is nearing its end. All of the internal quality controls have verified deliverables. A
flurry of client inspections has successfully resulted in sign-offs. However, you are having
trouble composing a report on the status of verified and accepted deliverables, and you have had
to make several calls to key stakeholders to verify what they accepted.
What is the most likely step that might have been missed?
Top of Form
- **A Updating the stakeholder engagement assessment matrix with the new engagement levels**
- **B Updating the requirements traceability matrix with the status of the requirements**
- **C Updating the roof-shaped matrix diagram with trade-offs**
- **D Updating the decision tree with the expected monetary value**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Wouldn't it be nice if all the requirements were listed in one place, along with the deliverables
that fulfill them, and the state of those requirements? Oh, wait. There is such a document!
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

The scenario implies that you have been conducting quality control and scope validation. If you
are having trouble tracking the status of requirements and deliverables, you are probably not
updating the requirements traceability matrix as necessary throughout the project life cycle. The

---

requirements traceability matrix is a grid that links product requirements from their origin to the
deliverables that satisfy them. Using this matrix throughout the project life cycle helps ensure
that each requirement adds business value by linking it to the business and project objectives.
Updates to the requirements traceability matrix are one of the outputs of the Validate Scope
process. Of the choices provided, updating the status of the requirements in the requirements
traceability matrix each time the linked deliverable is signed off by the stakeholders is what was
most likely missed in the scenario described.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Updating the stakeholder engagement assessment matrix with the new engagement levels**
Incorrect. The stakeholder engagement assessment matrix is a tool used in the Plan
Stakeholder Engagement process. The matrix shows the desired engagement levels but does
not specify the status of the requirements or the deliverables that satisfy them.
- **B Updating the requirements traceability matrix with the status of the requirements**
Correct. The requirements traceability matrix is a project document that links the product
requirements with the deliverables that satisfy them. This matrix should be updated every
time a requirement changes state, especially where the related deliverable(s) have been
internally verified and then client-accepted.
- **C Updating the roof-shaped matrix diagram with trade-offs**
Incorrect. A roof-shaped matrix diagram is an advanced quality management tool that can
show how column headings are all related to each other and may involve trade-offs in
implementation. A roof-shaped matrix has nothing to do with the requirements or
deliverables.
- **D Updating the decision tree with the expected monetary value**
Incorrect. A decision tree is a diagramming and calculation technique used in the Perform
Quantitative Risk Analysis process for evaluating the implications of a chain of multiple
options in the presence of uncertainty. This tool is not used to track deliverables,
requirements, or their acceptance.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 167

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 6
Top of Form
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 119 of 200
Question ID: 651336
The project keeps running into similar errors. The project manager is surprised, as she had plans
in place to mitigate these errors.
What is most likely the root cause of these errors?
Top of Form
- **A Incompetent project team members**
- **B Risk response plan not being implemented**
- **C Not enough meetings are held**
- **D Having repeating errors is normal for any project**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Why would a project use a mitigation strategy?
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

Mitigation is used in case of a negative risk where you try to optimize the chances of the project
meetings its objective by making the effects of a loss or risk less unpleasant, harmful, or serious.
In this scenario, a mitigation strategy was crafted for an identified project risk. As the project
progresses, the errors persist. Based on the information and options presented it appears the most
likely root cause is the risk response plan in not being implemented as planned. It is possible that

---

the mitigation plans are not effective, but the latter was not presented as one of the options in the
question.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Incompetent project team members**
Incorrect. Blaming the project team is not the root cause of the errors based on the limited
information presented.
- **B Risk response plan not being implemented**
Correct. Based on what is known in this scenario, there are known recurring issues that the
project has plans to mitigate. Nevertheless, the errors continue, which suggests that the risk
response plans are not working or they have not been implemented.
- **C Not enough meetings are held**
Incorrect. Even though meetings can be effective in addressing issues, the lack of meetings
is not the cause for errors to persist.
- **D Having repeating errors is normal for any project**
Incorrect. While errors can happen on any project, repeating errors indicate a problem that
should be investigated and resolved. Having repeating errors is not normal and may lead to
project failure.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 449-452

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 6
Top of Form
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 120 of 200
Question ID: 612814
- **A project’s supplier merges with one of its largest competitors. The new larger company issues a**
memo that states that they are honoring all existing contracts. The project manager determines
that the risks associated with the contract have been reduced by having a larger company as a
supplier.
What is the best course of action for the project manager?
Top of Form
- **A Remove all the risks associated with the original supplier from the risk register**
- **B Do nothing as all existing contracts remain unchanged**
- **C Update the procurement management plan with the details of the new supplier**
- **D Review the stakeholder register and revise it as necessary**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

There are new people who are affected by or may affect the project.
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

Any time there are changes with a vendor, it is important to ensure that the stakeholders and
contacts have not changed. Mergers are a prime example of where such a change can happen.
Hence, the project manager should review and update the stakeholder register. With the merger,
there are bound to be new stakeholders, and the project manager should review the stakeholder

---

register with existing procurement contracts to ensure the register is correct and complete. There
may very well be additional changes that need to be made to elements of the project management
plan, but the project manager needs first to analyze the situation to determine what changes are
needed. Therefore, of the choices provided, reviewing the stakeholder register is the best course
of action for the project manager.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Remove all the risks associated with the original supplier from the risk register**
Incorrect. According to the scenario, the project manager has determined that the risks
associated with this supplier have been reduced but not eliminated. Therefore, removing
'all' the risks for the original supplier from the risk register would be inappropriate.
- **B Do nothing as all existing contracts remain unchanged**
Incorrect. Although the contract is unchanged, there are other aspects of the project that
may be affected. For example, the merger will likely result in additional stakeholders to the
project. Once the changes are fully understood, the stakeholder engagement plan and
communications management plan, among others, may need to be updated. At the very
least, the project manager will need to analyze how the merger may impact the project and
its stakeholders.
- **C Update the procurement management plan with the details of the new supplier**
Incorrect. An update to any of the components of the project management plan, such as the
procurement management plan, requires an approved change request. But even with the
approved change request, the procurement management plan does not need to be updated
with the details of the new supplier since this information is not part of the plan.
- **D Review the stakeholder register and revise it as necessary**
Correct. With the merger, there are bound to be additional stakeholders or updates required
to the stakeholder register. The project manager should review and update the stakeholder
register to ensure it is correct and complete.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 510

Question 121 of 200
Question ID: 651337
- **A series of activities are not staying on schedule. The team member assigned to the activities is**
not responding to the project manager's emails. The team member works offsite and is never able
to attend status meetings.
What is the project manager's best action?
Top of Form
- **A Seek alternative methods of communication**
- **B Replace the team member with a more reliable team member**
- **C Send another email marked urgent and copy the team member's manager**
- **D Develop a project communications management plan**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Where is the breakdown?
Correct Answer: A

**Explanation:**

There appears to be a communication breakdown between the project manager and the project
team member. As the project manager manages the project communications, he or she must be
seeking ways to maintain and improve the project communications. That may require some
adjustments and flexibility to be more effectual.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Seek alternative methods of communication**
Correct. The current means of communicating is not working well. Seeking options may
improve the communications with the project team member.
- **B Replace the team member with a more reliable team member**
Incorrect. The issue is not the team member's work or productivity. The issue is the
communications between the team member and the project manager.
- **C Send another email marked urgent and copy the team member's manager**
Incorrect. The current communications do not appear to be effective. More ineffective
communication does not correct the issue.
- **D Develop a project communications management plan**
Incorrect. A project communications management plan already exists in some format but
the communications management plan needs improvement.

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 6
Top of Form
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 122 of 200
Question ID: 651434
- **A project manager wants to ensure that communications are properly managed on her project.**
Which of the following enterprise environmental factors should the project manager consider?
Top of Form
- **A Political climate**
- **B Active listening**
- **C Risk report**
- **D Change log**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Enterprise environmental factors are conditions not under the control of the project team.
Correct Answer: A

**Explanation:**

Enterprise environmental factors (EEFs) are conditions, not under the control of the project team,
that influence, constrain, or direct the project. EEFs can be either internal or external to the
performing organization. Social and cultural influences and issues are considered external EEFs.
The political climate, codes of conduct, ethics, and perceptions are examples of the social and
cultural influences and issues. In the context of the Manage Communications process described
by the scenario, organizational culture, political climate, and governance framework are among
the EEFs that can influence this process. Therefore, the political climate is the enterprise

---

environmental factor that the project manager should consider to ensure that communications are
properly managed on her project.
The incorrect answer choices are not considered EEFs.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Political climate**
Correct. The political climate is an enterprise environmental factor that falls under the
category of the social and cultural influences and issues. Political climate can influence the
way the communications are managed on a project.
- **B Active listening**
Incorrect. Active listening is an example of interpersonal and team skill. It is one of many
tools and techniques of Manage Communications, which is the process described in the
scenario. However, active listening is not an enterprise environmental factor.
- **C Risk report**
Incorrect. The risk report presents information on sources of overall project risk, together
with summary information on identified individual project risks. This information is
communicated to risk owners and other impacted stakeholders. While the risk report is an
input to the Manage Communications process implied by the scenario, the risk report is a
project document and not an enterprise environmental factor.
- **D Change log**
Incorrect. The change log is a comprehensive list of changes submitted during the project
and their current status. This document is used as an input to the Manage Communications
process suggested by the scenario to communicate changes to the stakeholders. However,
the question is asking to select the choice which represents an enterprise environmental
factor (EEF). The change log is a project document and not an EEF.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 383
Bottom of Form

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 6
Top of Form
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 123 of 200
Question ID: 612767
During the early stages of project initiation, a project manager needs to develop a list of
high-level risks, which will be included in a document to authorize the project.
What should the project manager do next?
Top of Form
- **A Allocate contingency reserves**
- **B Seek advice from an expert in risk identification**
- **C Carry out the Identify Risks process**
- **D Wait until the project is officially authorized**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

The project manager is assisting with the development of the project charter. Which tool or
technique can be used as part of this process?
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

The question suggests that the Develop Project Charter process is underway with the
development of the project charter. High-level risks are identified and included in the project
charter. The project charter, once it is finalized and approved by the project sponsor, formally
authorizes the project. One of the tools and techniques that may be used during the Develop
Project Charter process is expert judgment. Expertise should be considered from individuals or

---

groups with specialized knowledge of or training in risk identification. Seeking advice from an
expert in risk identification describes expert judgment.
The project as described in this scenario is still in initiation. The high-level risks that are
included in the project charter may then be confirmed and elaborated as part of the Identify Risks
process when the risk register is created.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Allocate contingency reserves**
Incorrect. Contingency reserves are funds allocated for risk response plans, which are
developed during project planning to address identified risks. According to the scenario,
the project is still in the initiation, and even the high-level risks have not yet been identified,
let alone specific risks, for which contingency reserves would have to be allocated.
- **B Seek advice from an expert in risk identification**
Correct. This answer choice describes expert judgment. Expertise should be considered
from individuals or groups with specialized knowledge of or training in risk identification.
- **C Carry out the Identify Risks process**
Incorrect. The Identify Risks process belongs to the Planning Process Group, while
according to the scenario the project is still in initiation.
- **D Wait until the project is officially authorized**
Incorrect. The project charter is the document, which formally authorizes the project. In the
situation presented in the question, the project manager should not simply wait. The project
manager should take action to develop a list of high-level risks, which not only will be
included in the project charter but need to be weighed out by the sponsor along with costs
vs. benefits to determine whether to proceed with the project.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 79

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 6
Top of Form
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 124 of 200
Question ID: 613334
- **A project manager is following the resource management plan and needs to gain a better**
understanding of the team members' preferences and aspirations in order to tailor individual
developmental activities.
What is the best course of action?
Top of Form
- **A Conduct a team assessment**
- **B Provide ability tests to the project team members**
- **C Perform a SWOT analysis**
- **D Schedule structured interviews with each team member**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

How might the project team members be provided an opportunity to express their preferences
and aspirations?
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

Individual and team assessments are tools that may be useful in the Develop Team process.
Individual and team assessment tools give the project manager and the project team insight into
areas of strengths and weaknesses. These tools help project managers assess team members'
preferences, aspirations, how they process and organize information, how they make decisions,

---

and how they interact with people. Various tools are available such as attitudinal surveys,
specific assessments, structured interviews, ability tests, and focus groups. Preferences and
aspirations will be unique for each individual and will require an assessment at the individual
level. Of the available answer choices, structured interviews are the best tool for each team
member to express their personal preferences and aspirations.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Conduct a team assessment**
Incorrect. Individual and team assessments are tools which may be used in support of the
Develop Team process. A team assessment may provide insight into the overall strengths
and weaknesses of the project team. However, to gain a better understanding of individual
preferences and aspirations, individual assessments, rather than team assessments, are a
preferred tool.
- **B Provide ability tests to the project team members**
Incorrect. An ability test may provide insight into individual competencies and uncover any
gaps in skillset. However, preferences and aspirations are independent of abilities.
Therefore, ability tests would not provide a better understanding of individual preferences
and aspirations.
- **C Perform a SWOT analysis**
Incorrect. A SWOT Analysis is an analysis of strengths, weaknesses, opportunities, and
threats of an organization, project, or option. Although not a tool commonly used in the
Develop Team process, it could be applied to understand the strengths, weaknesses,
opportunities, and threats of various training and development options. However, a SWOT
analysis does not provide insight into individual preferences and aspirations.
- **D Schedule structured interviews with each team member**
Correct. Preferences and aspirations will be unique for each individual and will require an
individual assessment. Structured interviews represent one of the various individual and
team assessment tools which may be used in support of the Develop Team process.
Structured interviews provide an opportunity for each team member to express their
personal preferences and aspirations, making this choice the best answer to the question
asked.

**Reference:**


---

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 342

PMP Exam 6

Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 125 of 200
Question ID: 612007
- **A company is experiencing exponential growth and will soon run out of space in their current**
production facility. A needs assessment has been completed to evaluate alternatives. One of the
options to support future growth is to build an expansion on to their existing production facility.
What should the company do next?
Top of Form
- **A Collect requirements and develop the project management plan**
- **B Understand the business goals and objectives to recommend proposals**
- **C Prepare the business case and benefits management plan**
- **D Perform the processes within the Initiating Process Group**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

After the needs assessment, what is still required to serve as an input to the development of the
project charter?
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

The business case is a documented economic feasibility study used to establish the validity of the
benefits of a selected component lacking sufficient definition, and that is used as a basis for the
authorization of further project management activities. The benefits management plan is the
documented explanation defining the processes for creating, maximizing, and sustaining the

---

benefits provided by a project or program. The business case and benefits management plan
comprise the business documents which are used as an input to create the project charter.
Pre-project work includes developing the needs assessment, business case, and benefits
management plan. The pre-project work should be completed before project initiation. The
question states that the needs assessment has already been completed; therefore, the next step is
to prepare the business case and benefits management plan.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Collect requirements and develop the project management plan**
Incorrect. Collecting requirements and developing the project management plan are
activities that take place during project planning. According to the scenario, the project has
not even been initiated yet.
- **B Understand the business goals and objectives to recommend proposals**
Incorrect. The needs assessment involves understanding business goals and objectives,
issues, and opportunities and recommending proposals to address them. The scenario states
that the needs assessment has already been completed. Therefore, this answer choice can
be eliminated.
- **C Prepare the business case and benefits management plan**
Correct. Pre-project work includes developing the needs assessment, business case, and
benefits management plan. The pre-project work should be completed before project
initiation. The question states that the needs assessment has already been completed;
therefore, the next step is to prepare the business case and benefits management plan.
- **D Perform the processes within the Initiating Process Group**
Incorrect. The Initiating Process Group includes the processes of Develop Project Charter
and Identify Stakeholders. Before these processes are performed, the pre-project work
should be completed.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 30, 33, 77; see also Benefits realization
management framework

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 6
Top of Form
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 126 of 200
Question ID: 625061
You are leading an agile software development project. During a sprint review, the customer
rejects the deliverables stating that the grade is acceptable but not the quality.
Of the following, which might be the best course of action?
Top of Form
- **A Add another developer to increase velocity**
- **B Remove some of the features and focus on quality for the next iteration**
- **C Increase the number of features for the next sprint**
- **D Introduce more rigorous testing during the next sprint to reduce bugs**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

- **A high level of defects is an example of poor quality.**
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

The question indicates that the grade of the product is acceptable, but the quality is poor.
'Quality' and 'grade' are not the same concepts and are often confused. Quality refers to "the
degree to which a set of inherent characteristics fulfill requirements" (ISO 9000 [18]). Grade as a
design intent is a category assigned to deliverables having the same functional use but different
technical characteristics. In this scenario, the quantity of features (grade) is acceptable while the
quality of the deliverables is poor, which may be represented by the number and/or severity of

---

defects. Therefore, of the available options, introducing more rigorous testing during the next
sprint to reduce bugs is the best course of action in this scenario. Note, the scenario indicates that
the project is lead by agile methods, where frequent quality and review steps are already
supposed to be built in throughout the project rather than the end of the project. However, it
seems that the current quality assurance activities have been insufficient. Hence, introducing
more rigorous testing from the next sprint onwards will likely help to address the issue.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Add another developer to increase velocity**
Incorrect. There is no information presented by the question to suggest that the project is
running behind schedule. The question indicates that there is an issue with the quality of
the product. Increasing velocity without taking any other action is not likely to improve the
quality of the deliverables.
- **B Remove some of the features and focus on quality for the next iteration**
Incorrect. While quality is an issue in this scenario, removing some of the features may not
be acceptable to the customer. Having a robust set of features is an example of a
higher-grade product. Reducing the number of features may make the grade unacceptable
regardless of what happens with quality.
- **C Increase the number of features for the next sprint**
Incorrect. The quantity of features is an example of the product grade. The question states
that the grade was acceptable but not the quality. Increasing the number of features,
without any other action, is not likely to improve the quality of the product.
- **D Introduce more rigorous testing during the next sprint to reduce bugs**
Correct. A high level of defects (commonly referred to as bugs in software) is an example of
poor quality. Introducing more rigorous testing should improve the quality of the product by
reducing the quantity and severity of the defects.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 274
Bottom of Form
