PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 6
Top of Form
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 174 of 200
Question ID: 612029
- **A project manager oversees a team consisting of a business analyst and three software**
developers. The team released a prototype to the customer for review and just finished gathering
new requirements for the next project iteration. After reviewing the requirements documentation,
the project manager discovers that some of the requirements were never documented.
In this scenario, who would be the person responsible for gathering and documenting business
requirements?
Top of Form
- **A The project manager**
- **B The customer**
- **C The business analyst**
- **D The developers**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Among the given choices, which role specializes in conducting business analysis?
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

On projects that have an assigned business analyst, eliciting, documenting and managing
stakeholder requirements is the responsibility of that role. The business analyst has the unique
skill set and expertise to do the requirements-related work, whereas the senior programmers

---

would likely be responsible for executing project deliverables to meet the business requirements.
The project manager may work closely with the business analyst, especially on such a small
project team, but is focused on overseeing the requirements management process and its
integration with the overall project. The project manager in this scenario is fulfilling that
responsibility by reviewing the requirements documentation, but it is the business analyst who is
responsible for gathering and documenting the business requirements.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A The project manager**
Incorrect. The project manager provides overall coordination and oversight of the
requirements management process. This includes ensuring that requirements-related work
is accounted for in the project management plan and ensuring that requirements-related
activities are performed on time and within budget and deliver value. However, it's the
business analyst who is responsible for analyzing, defining, documenting and managing
requirements.
- **B The customer**
Incorrect. The customer will likely provide the requirements to the performing organization.
However, it is the representative of the performing organization (the business analyst in the
scenario described) who is responsible for gathering and documenting business
requirements.
- **C The business analyst**
Correct. On projects with an assigned business analyst, requirements-related activities are
the responsibility of that role. The business analyst specializes in conducting business
analysis and is responsible for analyzing, defining, documenting and managing
requirements, while the project manager ensures that requirements-related activities are
accounted for in the project management plan and are performed on time and within
budget and deliver value.
- **D The developers**
Incorrect. For successful projects, there should be a clear delineation of roles and
responsibilities within the project team to avoid unnecessary confusion, overlap, or
inefficiency. The developers, as the name implies, are individuals who develop the product
based on the requirements collected and documented by a business analyst.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 132

PMP Exam 6

Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 175 of 200
Question ID: 613484
You are managing a proof-of-concept project that is developing a new tunnel boring machine. A
small-scale prototype has been designed and is undergoing a thorough test regime. During the
tests, your team discovers that the original test equipment will have to be updated with new
probes appropriate for the small prototype. This will substantially increase the cost of the project.
What is your next step?
Top of Form
- **A Have the team determine the full extent of the changes needed, and update the change**
management plan to reflect these changes
- **B Determine the full cost of new test gear, then find a way to hide the change by economizing in a**
variety of other activities
- **C Determine the cost of the new components, and submit a change request to update the cost**
baseline
- **D Review the requirements traceability matrix to determine why the appropriate cutting tooth alloy**
was not originally specified
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Find the best way to solve the problem and move the project forward.
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**


---

The question implies you are carrying out the Manage Quality process. The change in cost is the
specific impact highlighted in the scenario, so you need to address this proactively. First, the
actual cost difference must be determined, and then you need to follow the project's change
control process to modify the cost baseline. Ideally, the impact on all project constraints should
be analyzed to determine if other baselines or configurable elements need to be updated.
However, the scenario mentions only a cost increase. Therefore, of the available choices,
determining the cost of the new components and submitting a change request to update the cost
baseline is the best answer.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Have the team determine the full extent of the changes needed, and update the change**
management plan to reflect these changes
Incorrect. While it is appropriate to determine the full extent of the changes, the change
management plan does not need to be updated because this plan details how changes will
be managed rather than what changes have been requested.
- **B Determine the full cost of new test gear, then find a way to hide the change by**
economizing in a variety of other activities
Incorrect. The project manager is required by the PMI Code of Ethics and Professional
Conduct to operate with honesty and transparency at all times. Hiding the cost change for
the new gear is unethical behavior and will ultimately destroy trust in the project
organization.
- **C Determine the cost of the new components, and submit a change request to update the cost**
baseline
Correct. The change in cost is the specific impact highlighted, so you'll need to proactively
address this. First, the actual cost difference must be determined, and then you need to
follow the correct process to change the cost baseline. Note: if the issue has been identified
as a risk during project planning and a contingency reserve has been allocated for it, then
the cost baseline may not have to be updated. However, there is not enough information in
the question to make this determination.
- **D Review the requirements traceability matrix to determine why the appropriate cutting**
tooth alloy was not originally specified
Incorrect. Although the requirements traceability matrix may shed light on the original
requirements, the priority for the project manager is to identify the best path forward.

**Reference:**


---

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 297, 83, 254

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 6
Top of Form
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 176 of 200
Question ID: 613186
- **A project manager is in the process of identifying and categorizing stakeholders for a project**
with a large and complex community of stakeholders and needs to determine the relative
importance of the identified stakeholders.
What is the best course of action?
Top of Form
- **A Use a salience model to describe the classes of stakeholders**
- **B Review the agreements**
- **C Apply directions of influence to classify the stakeholders**
- **D Meet with all project stakeholders**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

How might the classes of stakeholders be described based on assessments of their power,
urgency, and legitimacy?
Correct Answer: A

**Explanation:**

The question implies that the project manager is performing the Identify Stakeholders process.
The salience model, an example of the data representation technique that can be used during this
process, describes classes of stakeholders based on assessments of their power, urgency, and
legitimacy. The salience model is useful for large complex communities of stakeholders

---

described in the scenario or where there are complex networks of relationships within the
community. The model is also useful in determining the relative importance of the identified
stakeholders which is what the question is asking, making the salience model the best answer to
the question.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Use a salience model to describe the classes of stakeholders**
Correct. The salience model describes classes of stakeholders based on assessments of
their power, urgency, and legitimacy, which is useful in determining the relative importance
of the identified stakeholders as asked by the question.
- **B Review the agreements**
Incorrect. The question does not indicate whether or not there are any existing agreements
at this point in the project. Even if agreements do exist, they may serve as a source of
stakeholders which need to be included in the stakeholder register, but reviewing the
agreements is not very helpful in determining the relative importance of the identified
stakeholders.
- **C Apply directions of influence to classify the stakeholders**
Incorrect. Directions of influence classify stakeholders according to their influence on the
work of the project or the project team itself. With the directions of influence model,
stakeholders are classified as upward, downward, outward, or sideward. Whereas, the
question is asking for a way to determine the relative importance of stakeholders rather
than a classification of their direction of influence.
- **D Meet with all project stakeholders**
Incorrect. Meetings are among the tools and techniques that can be used during the Identify
Stakeholder process described in the scenario. However, meeting with 'all' project
stakeholders seems unrealistic and is not the best use of the project manager's time,
especially when the project involves a large and complex community of stakeholders as
stated by the question.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 513

Question 177 of 200
Question ID: 651327
Services per the contract agreement with the vendor were delivered and signed off by the project
manager.
What else must the project manager do?
Top of Form
- **A Conduct a procurement audit**
- **B Close the procurement documents**
- **C Verify vendor scope**
- **D Notify customer on services received**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

What must be done if all procured services have been delivered and accepted?
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

Any procurement needs that are to be fulfilled by an outside party must have all the procurement
documents - e.g. agreements, contracts - formally closed once all services and/or products have
been delivered and accepted by the project. Additional procurement closure policies and
procedures may be outlined and defined in the procurement management plan.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Conduct a procurement audit**
Incorrect. A procurement audit is a structured review of the procurement process. The audit
can be used among the tools and techniques of the Control Procurements process.
Conducting a procurement audit is good practice for a project to review its procurement
procedures and process, but it is not mandatory, nor is it typically something performed by
the project manager.
- **B Close the procurement documents**
Correct. The project manager must close the corresponding procurement documents per the
services delivered and their agreements.
- **C Verify vendor scope**
Incorrect. Verifying the scope and the vendor's work is conducted prior to services
delivered and signed off.
- **D Notify customer on services received**
Incorrect. Informing the customer that your project received services from a third party
may be part of the project's communications plan, but that is not something that every
project 'must' do. There is no indication in the question that notification is a must in this
situation.

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 6

Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 178 of 200
Question ID: 612834
Your project team inspected a random sample of the work products. The resulting control chart
showed that any process variance was within acceptable limits. After additional testing, the
project team has reported that the deliverables have been verified.
What should your team do next?
Top of Form
- **A Create a scatter diagram and a Pareto histogram**
- **B Benchmark the samples against your competitors' products**
- **C Compare the work performance data to the scope baseline**
- **D Ask the customer if the deliverables meet their acceptance criteria**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Once the Control Quality process produces verified deliverables, they become an input to the
Validate Scope process.
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

The scenario implies the project team has completed the Control Quality process which has
resulted in verified deliverables as its output. After the deliverables have been verified internally,
they become an input to the Validate Scope process where they should be formally accepted by
the customer or sponsor. The customer or sponsor may inspect the deliverables, referring to the

---

requirements documentation, the scope baseline, the contract, or the statement of work for
requirements specifications. If the verified deliverables are found to be satisfactory, they are
accepted and become accepted deliverables as an output of the Validate Scope process.
Therefore, of the choices provided, after the deliverables have been verified, asking the customer
if the deliverables meet the customer's acceptance criteria is the next logical step for the project
team to take.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Create a scatter diagram and a Pareto histogram**
Incorrect. A scatter diagram and a Pareto histogram are among the tools of the Control
Quality process. Since the control chart did not find unacceptable variances, there is no
need to identify correlations between issues using the scatter diagram or prioritize issues
using the Pareto histogram.
- **B Benchmark the samples against your competitors' products**
Incorrect. Benchmarking is a data gathering tool used in several processes, such as Collect
Requirements, Plan Quality Management, and Plan Stakeholder Engagement. These
processes are part of the Planning Process Group, while the scenario describes a project in
execution.
- **C Compare the work performance data to the scope baseline**
Incorrect. This answer choice describes variance analysis which is a data analysis
technique used in the Control Scope process to analyze variances and trends in project and
product scope. The Control Scope process does not use the verified deliverables as its
input.
- **D Ask the customer if the deliverables meet their acceptance criteria**
Correct. After the deliverables have been verified internally by the project team during the
Control Quality process, they become an input to the Validate Scope process to be formally
accepted by the customer or sponsor. Therefore, asking the customer if the deliverables
meet their acceptance criteria is the best answer to the question asked.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 163-166

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 6

Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 179 of 200
Question ID: 625073
To help improve the communication of a virtual team, the project manager deploys an online
chat tool with channels for various topics that everyone uses while working. Often, all is quiet,
but sometimes, there are sudden long streams of chat about many topics, both related and
unrelated to the project work. The chat stream can be quite distracting, and it is often difficult to
find important points that relate to work.
What is the best course of action for the project manager?
Top of Form
- **A Nothing. Online chat is a release for people getting to know one another.**
- **B Eliminate the chat tool and instruct the team to use email and phone instead.**
- **C Join in on the fun and encourage the team to keep on with this type of conversation.**
- **D Request the team to use another channel for non-work related conversations.**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

The project manager needs to balance team building with the project work.
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

People need time to build relationships and learn about each other. There is a time a place for
relationship building and providing a way for casual conversation is important. To avoid
distracting the other team members, these off-topic conversations need to be incorporated in a

---

manner that does not interfere with project work. Establishing a separate channel for topics
unrelated to the project and politely asking the team members to use it, represents an appropriate
balance between the project work and team building.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Nothing. Online chat is a release for people getting to know one another.**
Incorrect. The question indicates that the off-topic conversations are distracting, which is
an issue that should be addressed. People need to use the tool to build and reinforce the
team, but they need to do it without impeding other communication.
- **B Eliminate the chat tool and instruct the team to use email and phone instead.**
Incorrect. It is important for the project team members to be able to establish positive
working relationships, and it is unrealistic to avoid some personal interactions. Replacing
the tool with email and phone is likely to be an ineffective approach and may even
demoralize the team. Additionally, neither email nor phone can prevent non-work related
conversations.
- **C Join in on the fun and encourage the team to keep on with this type of conversation.**
Incorrect. Too much conversation that is unrelated to work may annoy some people, causes
a distraction, and important information may be lost in the jocular banter.
- **D Request the team to use another channel for non-work related conversations.**
Correct. The project manager needs to establish a healthy balance between the project
work and team building. This approach represents a way to allow the project team
members to focus on the project work when needed and building positive working
relationships.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 384

Question 180 of 200
Question ID: 626002
You are new to the organization and have been given a few weeks to get yourself settled before
starting your project in a role of a project manager. During this period, you realize that you have
no authority over resources, the staff members are grouped by specialty, the budget is under the
full control of those group's managers, and you as a project manager are only required to
dedicate part of your time to perform the project work.
What type of an organization are you working in?
Top of Form
- **A Weak matrix**
- **B Functional**
- **C Balanced matrix**
- **D Projectized**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

In which type of organization does a project manager have no authority over resources?
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

Organizational structure can affect the availability of resources and influence how projects are
conducted. In a functional organization, the project manager's authority over resources is little to
none, the project budget is managed by the functional managers, and the project manager works

---

on project tasks part-time. Other project characteristics in a functional organization include little
to no resource availability and part-time project management administrative staff.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Weak matrix**
Incorrect. Even though in a weak matrix organization a project manager has low authority
over resources, it is still considered an authority that the project manager can use. The
scenario, however, describes no authority at all, making weak matrix an incorrect answer
choice.
- **B Functional**
Correct. In a functional organization, the project manager's authority over resources is
little to none, the project budget is managed by the functional manager, and the project
manager is working on project tasks part-time. Based on the scenario described, you are
working in a functional organization.
- **C Balanced matrix**
Incorrect. In a balanced matrix organization, the project manager's authority over
resources is low to moderate, and the project budget is managed by both the functional
manager and the project manager. The scenario describes no authority over resources and
the budget is managed by the functional manager.
- **D Projectized**
Incorrect. In a projectized organization, the project manager's authority over resources is
high to almost total, the project budget is managed by the project manager, and the project
manager is working on project tasks full-time. The scenario describes no authority over
resources, a budget that is managed by the functional manager, and the project manager
works on project tasks part-time.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 47

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 6
Top of Form
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 181 of 200
Question ID: 613230
You and your project team have recently discovered a negative risk to the project and determined
that it could result in a loss of $50,000 if it occurs. You have also determined that the probability
of this risk occurring is 50%.
What is the expected monetary value for this risk?
Top of Form
- **A $250,000**
- **B -$250,000**
- **C $25,000**
- **D -$25,000**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Calculate the expected monetary value for the threat of loss using the EMV formula.
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

You can calculate the expected monetary value of a risk by multiplying the impact amount by the
probability of occurrence. You would use a positive impact amount if the risk is a positive risk
(opportunity), and a negative impact amount if the risk is a negative risk (threat). In this scenario,
EMV = -$50,000 X 0.50 = -$25,000.

---


**Details for Each Option:**

- **A $250,000**
Incorrect. You may have gotten this answer if you did two things wrong: 1) neglected to
make the loss a negative number, and 2) multiplied the impact by the whole number 50,
instead of the decimal 0.50, which equals 50 percent.
- **B -$250,000**
Incorrect. You may have gotten this answer if you multiplied the impact by the whole
number 50, instead of the decimal 0.50, which equals 50 percent.
- **C $25,000**
Incorrect. You may have gotten this answer if you neglected to make the loss a negative
number.
- **D -$25,000**
Correct. To calculate EMV, multiply probability by impact, but remember that a loss should
be figured as a negative number. In this scenario, -50,000 * 0.50 = -$25,000

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 435

Question 182 of 200
Question ID: 613761
Your project team has just finished identifying potential project risks and is now scheduled to
conduct a risk workshop to begin categorizing and prioritizing those risks and assigning risk
owners. You decide to bring in a skilled facilitator to help lead the discussion. To enhance the
effectiveness of the workshop, the facilitator asks you to bring a few key project documents to
the meeting.
Which of the following documents would be the least valuable to bring?
Top of Form
- **A Milestone list**
- **B Assumption log**
- **C Risk register**
- **D Stakeholder register**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Which of the following answer choices is an input for quantitative risk analysis, rather than
qualitative risk analysis?
Correct Answer: A

**Explanation:**

The scenario describes a risk workshop, which is a technique used in the Perform Qualitative
Risk Analysis process. The risk register, stakeholder register, and assumption log are all project

---

documents that can be considered key inputs for that process and, therefore, would be valuable
resources to bring to the meeting. However, the milestone list is an input for the Perform
Quantitative Risk Analysis process which typically follows qualitative risk analysis. Therefore,
among the choices given, the milestone list the best answer to the question asked.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Milestone list**
Correct. The milestone list defines the schedule targets against which the results of a
'quantitative' schedule risk analysis are compared, in order to determine the confidence
level associated with achieving those targets. The scenario describes a risk workshop,
which is a technique used in 'qualitative' risk analysis. Therefore, of the answer choices
provided, the milestone list would be the least valuable document to bring to a meeting
focused on categorizing and prioritizing risks.
- **B Assumption log**
Incorrect. The assumption log is one of the key inputs for conducting a qualitative risk
analysis. The assumption log is used for identifying, managing, and monitoring key
assumptions and constraints that may affect the project. This information can be used in the
assessment of the priority of project risks.
- **C Risk register**
Incorrect. The risk register is one of the key inputs for conducting a qualitative risk
analysis. The risk register contains details of each identified project risk that will be
assessed during the Perform Qualitative Risk Analysis process.
- **D Stakeholder register**
Incorrect. The stakeholder register is one of the key inputs for conducting a qualitative risk
analysis. The stakeholder register includes details of project stakeholders who may be
selected as risk owners.

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 430, 421

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 6
Top of Form
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 183 of 200
Question ID: 613246
In an organization, project teams develop and follow their quality management plans. However,
almost all quality activities are focused on the effective use of project processes with very little
time spent on product design and process improvement.
What should you recommend to improve the way quality is approached in the organization?
Top of Form
- **A Focus on the quality assurance activities rather than on the Manage Quality process**
- **B Focus on the Manage Quality process rather than on quality assurance activities**
- **C Increase the budget allocated to team members for rewards and recognition**
- **D Outsource all quality management related activities to external vendors**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

What is the focus of quality assurance in project management?
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

The question implies that the project teams are performing the Manage Quality process. Manage
Quality is sometimes called quality assurance, although in project management Manage Quality
has a broader scope. Quality assurance is focused on the project processes and ensuring that they
are used effectively. Manage Quality includes all the quality assurance activities but is also
concerned with project design aspects and process improvements. According to the scenario,

---

almost all quality activities are focused on the effective use of project processes, with very little
time spent on product design and process improvement. This means only one area of the Manage
Quality process is covered. Therefore, to help the company to improve project quality, you
should recommend that their project teams cover all of these quality components by refocusing
on the Manage Quality process.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Focus on the quality assurance activities rather than on the Manage Quality process**
Incorrect. You are already focusing almost exclusively on quality assurance activities,
which is primarily about using project processes effectively.
- **B Focus on the Manage Quality process rather than on quality assurance activities**
Correct. The Manage Quality process includes all the quality assurance activities but is
also concerned with project design aspects and process improvements. By focusing on the
Manage Quality process, you cover all of these.
- **C Increase the budget allocated to team members for rewards and recognition**
Incorrect. Rewards and recognition are among the tools and techniques of the Develop
Team process used to encourage and support desirable behavior. There is not enough
information in the question to determine if there is a lack of rewards and recognition or to
ascertain if or how the team's behavior correlates with successfully managing quality.
- **D Outsource all quality management related activities to external vendors**
Incorrect. The quality management activities can be performed internally, externally, or as
a combination. However, it is the 'what' of the quality management content that determines
if the quality management on a project is adequate.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page 289

Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 184 of 200
Question ID: 612364
- **A project manager has been asked to draft a new project charter. The project manager has**
reviewed the existing agreements and studied the project business documents.
What might the project manager do next?
Top of Form
- **A Participate in the creation of the business case**
- **B Schedule a meeting with key stakeholders to identify summary information**
- **C Ask the project sponsor to formally authorize the project**
- **D Meet with key stakeholders to identify project risks and develop individual risk responses**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Which answer choice represents a tool or technique which may be useful in the development of
the project charter?
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

The question states that the project charter is the document currently under development. For the
creation of the project charter, meetings may be held with key stakeholders to identify the project
objectives, success criteria, key deliverables, high-level requirements, summary milestones, and
other summary information. The incorrect answer choices all represent actions that have either
already been completed or do not contribute to the development of the project charter. Therefore,

---

of the available options, scheduling a meeting with key stakeholders to identify summary
information is the best answer to the question asked.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Participate in the creation of the business case**
Incorrect. The question states that the project manager has already studied the project
business documents. The project business documents include the business case and the
benefits management plan. Therefore, the business case should have already been created
in this case.
- **B Schedule a meeting with key stakeholders to identify summary information**
Correct. For the creation of the project charter, meetings may be held with key stakeholders
to identify the project objectives, success criteria, key deliverables, high-level requirements,
summary milestones, and other summary information.
- **C Ask the project sponsor to formally authorize the project**
Incorrect. The project charter is the document which formally authorizes the existence of a
project. The question indicates that the project manager has just reviewed the existing
agreements and studied the project business documents, implying the project charter is in
its early development stages. The project charter must be completed before the project
sponsor can sign it off.
- **D Meet with key stakeholders to identify project risks and develop individual risk responses**
Incorrect. The project charter may include overall project risks but would not include
individual risk responses. Risks responses are not developed until the risk register is
created during project planning. The project in the scenario is still in initiating.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 80

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 6
Top of Form
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 185 of 200
Question ID: 625172
- **A project involves a diverse group of stakeholders and team members from different cultures all**
across the world. The project manager decides to use a social media tool to enhance
communications on the project. However, this would require everybody to create an account for
the tool to interact with others.
What is likely to be the biggest issue that the project manager will face?
Top of Form
- **A The cost of the tool may be so high that it would negate the benefits of using the tool**
- **B The fact that everyone uses different computers and mobile devices for access**
- **C Social media tools should never be allowed as a platform for project communications**
- **D Some project stakeholders and team members would be reluctant to use the tool**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Change can be difficult for some individuals.
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

Social media can be an effective tool for communication among stakeholders. Although social
media may be very prevalent in some regions, not all people embrace the use of social media,
especially when the stakeholders come from different cultures all across the world as described
by the scenario. Cultural awareness is an understanding of the difference between individuals,

---

groups, and organizations and adapting the project's communication strategy in the context of
these differences. While some of the project's stakeholders or team members may be interested in
using the social media tool, the requirement to create an account for the tool may be challenging
for others to get everyone engaged with the idea. Therefore, in this scenario, people's reluctance
to use the tool will likely be the biggest issue for the project manager.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A The cost of the tool may be so high that it would negate the benefits of using the tool**
Incorrect. While the question does not provide the specifics of the tool to be used, it is
unlikely that its cost would be so high to negate its benefits. Nowadays, there are many free
social media tools, and even those that have a charge are usually very affordable.
- **B The fact that everyone uses different computers and mobile devices for access**
Incorrect. Most social media applications are compatible with various platforms to ensure
widespread adoption. The fact that the stakeholders use different computers and mobile
devices is not likely to be a significant issue.
- **C Social media tools should never be allowed as a platform for project communications**
Incorrect. Although some companies may not allow the use of social media tools, these
tools have been used successfully on many projects. In recent years, companies have begun
to embrace social media as an effective communication tool. Absolute statements, such as
"never", "always", etc. typically represent incorrect answers.
- **D Some project stakeholders and team members would be reluctant to use the tool**
Correct. Since the group is diverse, some people may not feel comfortable using social
media for communications. Gaining broad acceptance of the tool will likely be the project
manager's biggest challenge.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 376, 383, 386

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 6
Top of Form
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 186 of 200
Question ID: 612648
You are currently in the process of determining and documenting the requirements for a project.
During this process, which of the following activities are you least likely to conduct?
Top of Form
- **A Glean any relevant information from the project charter**
- **B Use the stakeholder register to identify stakeholders that can provide information on**
requirements
- **C Gain an understanding of required, desired, and optional criteria for meeting the business needs**
- **D Determine how requirements activities will be planned, tracked, and reported**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Which of the answer choices describes an activity which is more likely to be performed as part
of the Plan Scope Management process rather than the Collect Requirements process?
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

Collect Requirements is the process of determining, documenting, and managing stakeholder
needs and requirements to meet objectives. Thus, the question implies that the Collect
Requirements process is being performed in this scenario. However, the question is asking to
select an activity which is 'least' likely to be conducted during the Collect Requirements process.
The incorrect answer choices describe the inputs into the Collect Requirements process. The

---

choice that describes how requirements activities will be planned, tracked, and reported is
captured in the requirements management plan, which is produced as an output of the Plan Scope
Management process and not the Collect Requirements process, making this choice the best
answer to the question asked.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Glean any relevant information from the project charter**
Incorrect. The question implies that the Collect Requirements process is being performed.
The project charter serves as an input into the Collect Requirements process and
documents the high-level description and high-level requirements that will be used to
develop detailed requirements.
- **B Use the stakeholder register to identify stakeholders that can provide information on**
requirements
Incorrect. The question describes the Collect Requirements process. The stakeholder
register is one of the inputs which may be beneficial for the Collect Requirements process.
The stakeholder register is used to identify stakeholders who can provide information on
the requirements.
- **C Gain an understanding of required, desired, and optional criteria for meeting the business**
needs
Incorrect. The question suggests that the Collect Requirements process is underway. A
business document that can influence the Collect Requirements process is the business
case, which can describe required, desired, and optional criteria for meeting the business
needs.
- **D Determine how requirements activities will be planned, tracked, and reported**
Correct. This answer choice describes an element of the requirements management plan.
The requirements management plan is created as part of the Plan Scope Management
process rather than the Collect Requirements process.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 137, 138, 140-141

Question 187 of 200
Question ID: 612811
You are in the process of determining stakeholder needs and requirements for the project you are
leading. There is a large number of stakeholders who are geographically dispersed, and you need
their inputs quickly.
What tool or technique would be the most effective in this situation?
Top of Form
- **A Face-to-face meeting**
- **B Decision making**
- **C Alternatives analysis**
- **D Questionnaires**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

This method is used as a tool of the Collect Requirements process; it needs to be quick and cover
a large group of people.
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

The scenario implies you are involved in the Collect Requirements process. This process is
performed to determine, document, and manage stakeholder needs and requirements to meet
project objectives. Questionnaires and surveys are an example of a data gathering technique that
can be used as part of this process. Questionnaires and surveys are written sets of questions

---

designed to quickly accumulate information from a large number of respondents. Questionnaires
and/or surveys are most appropriate with varied audiences when a quick turnaround is needed
and when the respondents are geographically dispersed.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Face-to-face meeting**
Incorrect. The question is asking about the most effective method to use with a large
number of stakeholders who are geographically dispersed. Since you need the stakeholders'
input quickly, gathering all stakeholder in a face-to-face meeting seems unrealistic.
- **B Decision making**
Incorrect. Decision making is a technique that can be used to select a course of action from
different alternatives. According to the scenario, your goal is to collect requirements for the
project rather than make a decision.
- **C Alternatives analysis**
Incorrect. An alternative analysis is a technique used to evaluate identified options in order
to select approaches to use to execute and perform the work of the project. The scenario
does not describe options to select from.
- **D Questionnaires**
Correct. Questionnaires and surveys are written sets of questions designed to accumulate
information from a large number of respondents quickly. This method is used effectively
with a large number of stakeholders who are geographically dispersed, making this choice
the best answer the question asked.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 143

Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 188 of 200
Question ID: 612012
You have just taken over a project in which some of the deliverables will be produced by
external vendors. You want to familiarize yourself with those who are involved in the project
from the sellers' side.
Where would you look to obtain this information?
Top of Form
- **A Bid documents**
- **B Stakeholder register**
- **C Seller proposals**
- **D Stakeholder engagement plan**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

What document contains specific information about stakeholders that may be impacted by or that
could impact the project?
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

The stakeholder register is a project document that contains relevant information regarding
stakeholder interests, involvement, interdependencies, influence, and potential impact on project
success. Vendors are project stakeholders and as such should be included in the stakeholder
register. The project manager and project team members should refer to this document when

---

obtaining pertinent information about project stakeholders whether the stakeholders are internal
or external to the performing organization.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Bid documents**
Incorrect. Bid documents are used to solicit proposals from prospective sellers. Bid
documents do not contain information about those who are involved in the project from the
sellers' side.
- **B Stakeholder register**
Correct. The stakeholder register contains details about the identified project stakeholders,
including sellers. This information includes stakeholder identification information,
assessment information, and stakeholder classification.
- **C Seller proposals**
Incorrect. Seller proposals are the documents prepared by the prospective sellers in
response to bid documents. While seller proposals contain some of the information about
the sellers, this information does not provide the details that would allow you to familiarize
with those who are involved in the project from the sellers' side. Additionally, responses are
received from all sellers interested in the bid while eventually some of them would not be
selected making some of the seller responses irrelevant.
- **D Stakeholder engagement plan**
Incorrect. The stakeholder engagement plan is a component of the project management
plan that identifies the strategies required to promote the involvement of stakeholders in
decision making on and execution of the project. While sellers are project stakeholders,
information about them is not included in the stakeholder engagement plan.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 514

Question 189 of 200
Question ID: 612074
You are working with your project team to identify and document the specific actions to be
performed to produce the project deliverables.
Which of the following do you need before you can start this process?
Top of Form
- **A Scope baseline**
- **B Issue log**
- **C Risk register**
- **D Activity list**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Which of the following is an input to the Define Activities process?
Correct Answer: A

**Explanation:**

To answer this question correctly, you should determine what process is being described.
Identifying and documenting the specific actions to be performed to produce the project
deliverables is the definition of the Define Activities process. The question asks, "Which of the
following do you need before you can start this process?" In other words, the question asks
which of the following answer choices represents an input to the Define Activities process. Of

---

the choices provided, only the scope baseline is one of the inputs to the Define Activities
process.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Scope baseline**
Correct. You are in the Define Activities process, which involves decomposing work
packages into the activities required to produce them. The required inputs are the schedule
management plan, the scope statement, the work breakdown structure (WBS), and the WBS
dictionary. These last three documents make up the scope baseline.
- **B Issue log**
Incorrect. The issue log is a project document where information about issues is recorded
and monitored. According to the scenario, the project is still in planning, while the issue
log is typically created for the first time during project execution as an output of the Direct
and Manage Project Work process.
- **C Risk register**
Incorrect. The risk register is a repository in which the outputs of risk management
processes are recorded. The scenario describes the Define Activities process and asks to
select the answer choice that represents one of the inputs to the process. The risk register is
not an input to the Define Activities process.
- **D Activity list**
Incorrect. The activity list is a comprehensive list that includes all schedule activities
required on the project. It is an output of the Define Activities process implied by the
scenario, not an input to the process. You first need to go through the process of
decomposition; therefore, this choice is incorrect.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 184, 161

Question 190 of 200
Question ID: 613178
- **A project manager and team lead meet with the customer to discuss project progress. The project**
manager notices that when the team lead communicates with the customer, she tends to mirror
the customer’s body language. Nearly every time the customer folds their arms, sits back in their
chair, or puts their hands together on the table, so does the team lead.
What should the project manager do?
Top of Form
- **A In private, tell the team lead stop mocking the customer**
- **B Call this behavior to the team lead attention and apologize to the customer**
- **C Do nothing. There is nothing wrong with the team lead's behavior**
- **D Establish communication classes for the project team**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

The question describes a communication concept called mirroring.
Correct Answer: C

**Explanation:**

The question describes a communication concept called mirroring. When two people are
communicating well, they will often subconsciously mirror the other person's behavior and body
language. This action is typically a sign of a comfortable conversation. The project manager
should do nothing in this scenario as there is no issue to correct. Note that "do nothing" is

---

typically used as an incorrect answer choice, but this may not always be the case. In some
circumstances, taking no action is the most appropriate approach.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A In private, tell the team lead stop mocking the customer**
Incorrect. There is no information presented by the question to suggest that the team lead is
mocking the customer. Mirroring can be a normal reaction when connecting with another
person.
- **B Call this behavior to the team lead attention and apologize to the customer**
Incorrect. The question does not suggest there is anything wrong with the team lead
behavior. More importantly, it would be inappropriate to correct her behavior in front of
the customer.
- **C Do nothing. There is nothing wrong with the team lead's behavior**
Correct. When two people are connecting in a conversation, they quite often subconsciously
mirror the other person’s behavior.
- **D Establish communication classes for the project team**
Incorrect. Although communication classes may or may not benefit the team, the question
does not imply that a communication issue exists to justify this action.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 384

PMP Exam 6
Top of Form
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 191 of 200
Question ID: 651326
The software release update has been developed and is scheduled for the switch over to the live
environment at midnight tomorrow. Per the agreement, the closing of the project requires
knowledge sharing and end-user readiness in coordination with the product launch.
Which of the following best represents these closing activities?
Top of Form
- **A Communicating project status to the sponsor; issuing the final report; notifying the project team**
of release readiness
- **B Training end users in the receiving organization; finalizing documentation; conducting final**
readiness assessments
- **C Backing up software files; uploading project documents to PMO repository; verifying all asset**
management records
- **D Communicating the project status to the end users; releasing the project team; verifying product**
completion
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Which list offers the most opportunities to move knowledge from the project team to the owners
of the outcome?
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**


---

As a project is transferring the ownership and operation of the project's product to another team
or the customer, transferring knowledge is important. This transference is not exclusively
collecting the knowledge and handing it over. It requires training, educating, and communicating
the contents, organization, and purpose of the knowledge and associated wisdom to the receiving
entity.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Communicating project status to the sponsor; issuing the final report; notifying the project**
team of release readiness
Incorrect. Communication is important, but it is not the sole means of knowledge transfer,
especially when that communication is only internal and not to those who are to own that
knowledge moving forward. The three activities listed in this answer choice are internal to
the project organization.
- **B Training end users in the receiving organization; finalizing documentation; conducting**
final readiness assessments
Correct. Knowledge transfer requires some form of training and documentation. This list is
not complete but is the most comprehensive of those provided, making it the best answer to
the question asked.
- **C Backing up software files; uploading project documents to PMO repository; verifying all**
asset management records
Incorrect. Collecting and making knowledge accessible is an important first step to
knowledge sharing, but it is not enough on its own. Knowledge transfer requires
information on how to access and use the collected knowledge.
- **D Communicating the project status to the end users; releasing the project team; verifying**
product completion
Incorrect. The status of the project is typically communicated to the project stakeholders
rather than the end users. Verifying the product completion is not transferring the
knowledge, but validating the scope and that the work was done. Releasing the project team
before knowledge is transferred to the receiving organization may be a premature action.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 127

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 6
Top of Form
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 192 of 200
Question ID: 612735
- **A project manager goes into the monthly steering committee meeting and says the project has a**
cost variance of $25,378.22. Instead of being praised for running under budget, one of the
executives at the meeting expresses frustration at the number.
What is wrong with the variance?
Top of Form
- **A The variance was calculated incorrectly.**
- **B The level of precision is not correct.**
- **C The variance is greatly exaggerated.**
- **D The variance should be a negative value.**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Do pennies really mean that much?
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

The level of precision for costs is defined in the cost management plan and can be described as
the degree to which costs estimates will be rounded up or down, based on the scope of the

---

activities and magnitude of the project. Reporting a cost variance to the penny implies a level of
precision that is not realistic, as the project's cost variance is constantly changing. Additionally,
although the money spent might be obtained for any point in a project, the earned value needed
to calculate the cost variance is more subjective. Therefore, providing a cost variance to the
penny implies a level of precision that is not obtainable. In this case, it would be more
appropriate to report the cost variance as $25,000.
As an analogy, imagine if a scientist stated that a particular dinosaur bone was 100,000,127 years
old. However, the test used to determine the age may only be accurate to a few million years.
Stating the age to the exact number of years implies that the scientist has determined the age to
an exact year when that is not the case, regardless of the test results.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A The variance was calculated incorrectly.**
Incorrect. There is not enough information presented in the scenario to determine whether
or not the variance was calculated correctly.
- **B The level of precision is not correct.**
Correct. Most projects have a level of precision that would round the variance rather than
report a cost variance to the penny. For example, $25,000 would be a more reasonable
number.
- **C The variance is greatly exaggerated.**
Incorrect. There is no information provided in the question to indicate that the extent of the
variance in cost is exaggerated.
- **D The variance should be a negative value.**
Incorrect. A variance can be negative, positive, or zero. Positive variances are generally an
indication that a project is running under planned costs, as described in the question.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 238
Bottom of Form

Question 193 of 200
Question ID: 612292
- **A project manager is drafting a charter for a software development project. In support of this**
process, the project manager has scheduled a brainstorming meeting to gather relevant
information.
Which of the following activities is the project manager least likely to conduct?
Top of Form
- **A Inviting relevant stakeholders to attend the meeting**
- **B Ensuring that a software engineer joins the meeting**
- **C Arranging for a facilitator to lead the meeting**
- **D Following the communications management plan to determine meeting attendees**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Which answer choice represents an activity that can only occur later in the project?
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

The question states that the project charter is being developed, which occurs during project
initiation. Brainstorming is a data gathering technique which may be useful in the development
of the project charter. Brainstorming is a specialized meeting led by a facilitator which can be
used to gather data and solutions or ideas from stakeholders, subject matter experts, and team
members when developing the project charter. Note, the question is asking for the activity which

---

is 'least' likely to be conducted during the development of the project charter. The
communications management plan is not created until later in the project during the Plan
Communications Management process. Therefore, the project manager would not be able to
follow the communications management plan in determining the meeting attendees, making this
the 'least' likely activity to be conducted in this scenario.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Inviting relevant stakeholders to attend the meeting**
Incorrect. A stakeholder is an individual, group, or organization that may affect, be affected
by, or perceive itself to be affected by a decision, activity, or outcome of a project. Since
stakeholders have a vested interest in the project, it may be beneficial to seek their feedback
to incorporate into the project charter.
- **B Ensuring that a software engineer joins the meeting**
Incorrect. A software engineer can be considered a subject matter expert. Since the project
in this scenario involves software development, a software engineer will be able to provide
technical insights that may influence the development of the project charter.
- **C Arranging for a facilitator to lead the meeting**
Incorrect. A brainstorming session is conducted in a group environment. To ensure the
meeting is run effectively and kept on track, arranging for a facilitator to lead the meeting
is likely to be one of the actions taken by the project manager.
- **D Following the communications management plan to determine meeting attendees**
Correct. The question states that the project charter is being developed which occurs
during project initiation. The communications management plan is not created until later in
the project during the Plan Communications Management process.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 80

PMP Exam 6

Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 194 of 200
Question ID: 612155
You are attempting to coordinate activities between your project, another related project, and
operations, all of which are being managed as a group. A conflict has arisen over control of a key
resource that is vital to both projects as well as operations. The conflict has reached an impasse
and needs to be resolved by a higher authority.
What is your best course of action?
Top of Form
- **A Discuss the problem with the portfolio manager**
- **B Escalate the issue to the operations manager**
- **C Raise the issue with the other project manager**
- **D Request help from the project management office**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Which role has direct responsibility for projects, programs, and operations?
Correct Answer: A

**Explanation:**

The question describes a situation where a problem needs to be addressed by someone that is
responsible for projects, programs, and operations being managed as a group. A portfolio is a
collection of projects, programs, and operations managed as a group to achieve strategic
objectives. Only a portfolio manager has direct responsibility for projects, programs, and

---

operations. Therefore, discussing the problem with the portfolio manager is the best course of
action in this scenario.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Discuss the problem with the portfolio manager**
Correct. The question suggests that the conflict needs to be addressed by someone that is
responsible for projects, programs, and operations. Only a portfolio manager has direct
responsibility for all three of these areas.
- **B Escalate the issue to the operations manager**
Incorrect. Based on the scenario, the conflict has reached an impasse, which implies that
further discussion with the operations manager will not resolve the issue. Additionally, the
question indicates that the conflict will need to be escalated to someone with authority over
projects and operations, and an operations manager is not likely to have authority for
project execution.
- **C Raise the issue with the other project manager**
Incorrect. The question states that the conflict is at an impasse, which suggests that further
discussion with the other project manager is futile. Additionally, the question implies that
the issue needs to be escalated to someone with authority over projects, programs, and
operations being managed as a group. A project manager is not likely to oversee programs
and operations as part of their regular duties.
- **D Request help from the project management office**
Incorrect. The project management office (PMO) is a management structure that
standardizes the project-related governance processes and facilitates the sharing of
resources, methodologies, tools, and techniques. While the PMO may help (depending on
its role in the organization) with settling the conflict between the projects, the PMO would
unlikely have the authority over operations.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 13

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 6
Top of Form
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 195 of 200
Question ID: 612709
- **A large and complex multinational project is underway with stakeholders of diverse cultures and**
ages. The project manager has experienced issues communicating with such a diverse
stakeholder community.
What is the best course of action?
Top of Form
- **A Take a multifaceted approach to communication**
- **B Rely on push forms of communication**
- **C Utilize pull communications exclusively**
- **D Use interactive communication for all project communications**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

No single method of communication will be appropriate for all stakeholders and circumstances.
Correct Answer: A

**Explanation:**

Multifaceted approaches to communication represent one of the trends and emerging practices in
Project Communications Management. Multifaceted approaches to communication embrace and
select from all technologies and respect cultural, practical, and personal preferences for
language, media, content, and delivery. When appropriate, social media and other advanced
computing technologies may be included. Multifaceted approaches such as these are more

---

effective for communicating with stakeholders from different generations and cultures. The
incorrect answer choices represent limitations in the methods of communication, which may not
be appropriate for all stakeholders and circumstances. Therefore, of the available choices, the
best course of action is for the project manager to take a multifaceted approach to
communication.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Take a multifaceted approach to communication**
Correct. Multifaceted approaches to communication embrace and select from all
technologies and respect cultural, practical, and personal preferences for language, media,
content, and delivery. Multifaceted approaches are more effective for communicating with
stakeholders from different generations and cultures.
- **B Rely on push forms of communication**
Incorrect. Push communication is sent or distributed directly to the specific recipients who
need to receive the information. In this scenario, push communications should be utilized
along with other methods of communication to satisfy a diverse stakeholder community.
The project manager should not just rely on push communications.
- **C Utilize pull communications exclusively**
Incorrect. Pull communication is used for large complex information sets, or for large
audiences, and requires the recipients to access content at their own discretion. In this
scenario, pull communications should be utilized along with other methods of
communication to satisfy a diverse stakeholder community. However, the project manager
should not use pull communications exclusively.
- **D Use interactive communication for all project communications**
Incorrect. Interactive communication involves communication between two or more parties
performing a multidirectional exchange of information in real time. Interactive
communication may not be appropriate for large audiences or large information sets. It
would be unrealistic to use interactive communication for all project communications on a
large and complex project.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 364, 374
Bottom of Form

Question 196 of 200
Question ID: 651339
Due to the complexity and many diverse teams involved, there is confusion amongst the project
stakeholders on where to find materials and information for the project.
What is the best response to address this issue?
Top of Form
- **A Assign one project team member to retain and distribute all the project materials and information**
to have a single point of contact.
- **B Distribute all the project documents, materials, and updates to each stakeholder**
- **C Require all stakeholders to attend every meeting to ensure everyone receives the handouts and**
information
- **D Set up an information management system to store, share, and codify the project's knowledge**
and content
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Stakeholders are not able to locate project materials and information.
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**

As a project progresses, there can be a lot of information and systems - especially in a large,
complex project with many stakeholders. The root issue in this scenario is the inability of
stakeholders to locate the materials and the information they need. Building up the information

---

management tools would assist the project stakeholders to access and locate the information
needed or requested. All other options describe infeasible, counterproductive, or unmanageable
responses.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Assign one project team member to retain and distribute all the project materials and**
information to have a single point of contact.
Incorrect. Due to the complexity of the project, this solution is infeasible and
unmanageable.
- **B Distribute all the project documents, materials, and updates to each stakeholder**
Incorrect. Not every stakeholder needs every document, material, and constant updates.
This arrangement would be overwhelming and counterproductive.
- **C Require all stakeholders to attend every meeting to ensure everyone receives the handouts**
and information
Incorrect. Diverse teams are considered with different parts of the projects. Requiring
attendance at all meetings may help some stakeholders, but most meetings likely prove to
be counterproductive and time consuming for many stakeholders.
- **D Set up an information management system to store, share, and codify the project's**
knowledge and content
Correct. At its root, the project stakeholders need to access and locate project information.
Building up information management efforts would address this issue.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 103-104

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 6
Top of Form
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 197 of 200
Question ID: 613532
You are one of several project managers working for a construction company, and you are
obtaining the equipment and supplies for a project to build a new convention center. The
performing organization owns much of the construction equipment, which must be reserved in
advance per company policy.
Once you have confirmed the equipment's availability for your project, what should you do to
ensure the equipment is available when you need it?
Top of Form
- **A Revise the resource requirements documentation**
- **B Reserve the equipment by updating the organizational process assets**
- **C Modify the project schedule with the required equipment**
- **D Record the equipment in the resource breakdown structure**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

Reserving a resource requires coordination among the various project managers.
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

The question implies that you, as the project manager, are carrying out the Acquire Resources
process. Organizational process assets that are updated as a result of the Acquire Resources
process include documentation related to acquiring, assigning, and allocating resources.

---

Depending on how company policies and procedures govern the assignment of company
resources to projects, an organizational process assets update may be required to reserve a
resource. Examples of organizational process assets that might serve this purpose might include
an electronic sign-up sheet, an organizational level resource calendar which reflects all of the
individual project resource calendars, resource management software, a master schedule of all
projects, etc. The incorrect answer choices reflect project documents that only influence the
project for which they have been created, and not the other projects being conducted by the
performing organization. Therefore, of the available choices, reserving the equipment as an
organizational process assets update is the best answer to the question asked.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Revise the resource requirements documentation**
Incorrect. Resource requirements documentation is updated to reflect resources acquired
for the current project. However, updating the resource requirements documentation for
your will not influence other projects and would not reserve the construction equipment for
your project.
- **B Reserve the equipment by updating the organizational process assets**
Correct. Organizational process assets that are updated as a result of the Acquire
Resources process include documentation related to acquiring, assigning, and allocating
resources. Depending on how company policies and procedures govern the assignment of
company resources to projects, an organizational process assets update may be required to
reserve the required resources.
- **C Modify the project schedule with the required equipment**
Incorrect. Changes in the project schedule may result from the availability of required
resources. However, the project schedule will not likely influence all of the other projects
that are being conducted by the performing organization.
- **D Record the equipment in the resource breakdown structure**
Incorrect. The resource breakdown structure is a hierarchical representation of resources
by category and type. Resources that have been acquired are recorded in the resource
breakdown structure. However, recording the equipment for the project in the resource
breakdown structure will not reserve the resource for your project since this equipment
belongs to the organization and may be used by other projects unless the organizational
process assets specify to which project the equipment is reserved.

**Reference:**


---

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 335
Bottom of Form

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 6
Top of Form
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 198 of 200
Question ID: 626004
You are managing a large project with several major deliverables with deadlines spread over
time. Each deliverable has a distinct focus. The project involves different organizations, locations
and skill sets. You anticipate that you will use processes from all five process groups. Once a
deliverable is completed and handed over to the customer, a decision on whether to continue or
terminate the project should be made.
What approach would work best for this project?
Top of Form
- **A Outsource each deliverable to a different vendor**
- **B Do not undertake the project**
- **C Use Agile as it works best for large projects**
- **D Divide the project into phases**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

This project structure approach allows the project to be segmented into logical subsets for ease of
management, planning, and control.
Correct Answer: D

**Explanation:**


---

When the nature of the work to be performed is unique to a portion of the project, and each
portion can be linked to the development of a specific major deliverable, phased project
approach can be used. Typically, dividing the project into phases works best when:
 The work has a distinct focus that differs from any other phase. This often involves different
organizations, location, and skill sets;
 Achieving the primary deliverable or objective of the phase requires controls or processes unique to
the phase or its activities;
 The close of a phase ends with some form of transfer or hand-off of the work product produces as
the phase deliverable. This phase end represents a natural point to reassess the activities underway and
to change or terminate the project if necessary.
The project characteristics described in the question are covered by the above points. Therefore,
dividing the project into phases is the best answer among the choices given.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Outsource each deliverable to a different vendor**
Incorrect. There is not enough information in the question to determine whether
outsourcing each deliverable to a different vendor would work better than producing
everything in-house.
- **B Do not undertake the project**
Incorrect. The question states that you are already managing the project. Therefore,
suggesting not to undertake the project makes no sense.
- **C Use Agile as it works best for large projects**
Incorrect. The size of a project alone should not determine which methods should be
applied to a project. Agile is not a silver bullet and may or may not work for a large
project.
- **D Divide the project into phases**
Correct. All the project characteristics described in the scenario suggest that dividing the
project into phases would be the best approach to take among the answer choices provided.

**Reference:**


---

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 20-21
Bottom of Form

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 6
Top of Form
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 199 of 200
Question ID: 612647
Halfway through a project, the project sponsor left the organization, and a new sponsor was
appointed. You meet with the project sponsor to bring her up to speed and ensure she has the
appropriate level of support for the project. The new sponsor is excited about the project, and she
decides to expand the project slightly.
What should you do first?
Top of Form
- **A Submit a change request to expand the existing project**
- **B Terminate the existing project and initiate the expanded one**
- **C Request additional funds for the project**
- **D Update the work breakdown structure (WBS)**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

The project sponsor wants to modify the scope baseline.
Correct Answer: A

**Explanation:**

The question describes a situation in which the project sponsor is requesting an expansion of the
project scope. In addition to the scope baseline, this change will likely impact the cost and
schedule baselines as well. An approved change request is required to modify any of the project
baselines. Additionally, even though the project sponsor wields great power and influence, the

---

sponsor may not be the sole decision-maker. The configuration management plan will describe
what approvals are necessary to approve the change request, but it is likely that others will be
involved in this decision as well. Therefore, of the available choices, the first thing for the
project manager to do in this situation is to submit a change request.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Submit a change request to expand the existing project**
Correct. The question describes a situation in which the project scope is being expanded.
An approved change request is required to modify any of the project baselines.
- **B Terminate the existing project and initiate the expanded one**
Incorrect. Terminating a project and starting a new project is an option but does not make
much sense in this scenario. The question states that the project is already halfway
complete and the project sponsor wants to expand the project slightly. It would be more
practical to just expand the existing project rather than terminating it and starting a new
one.
- **C Request additional funds for the project**
Incorrect. An approved change request will be required to expand the project, which will
likely include a request for additional funds.
- **D Update the work breakdown structure (WBS)**
Incorrect. The WBS is a hierarchical decomposition of the total scope of work to be carried
out by the project team to accomplish the project objectives and create the required
deliverables. The WBS is a component of the scope baseline. An approved change request is
required to modify a baseline.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 528
Bottom of Form

PMP Exam Simulator
PMP Exam 6
Top of Form
Filtered Mode: Displaying 200 questions
Question 200 of 200
Question ID: 625025
- **A project manager is about to start the processes associated with the Initiating Process Group.**
The project manager needs to know who will be responsible for ensuring that the value to the
project is preserved a year after the project deliverables are handed over to the customer.
Where will the project manager find this information?
Top of Form
- **A Business case**
- **B Benefits management plan**
- **C Stakeholder register**
- **D Project charter**
Question answered incorrectly

**Hint:**

The business documents are likely the only project artifacts that exist at this point.
Correct Answer: B

**Explanation:**

The question states that the project is about to start the processes associated with the Initiating
Process Group. Hence, the only project artifacts that likely exist at this point are the business
documents, which include the business case and the benefits management plan. To find out who
will be responsible for value and benefits monitoring a year after the project provides the
deliverables, the project manager needs to turn to the benefits management plan. The benefits

---

management plan contains the details of the process for creating, maximizing, and sustaining the
benefits provided by a project. Therefore, of the available responses, the benefits management
plan is the best answer to the question asked.

**Details for Each Option:**

- **A Business case**
Incorrect. The business case is a documented economic feasibility study used to establish
the validity of the benefits of a selected component lacking sufficient definition and that is
used as a basis for the authorization of further project management activities. The business
case is not likely to have details regarding maximizing the value of project deliverables
after they have been delivered.
- **B Benefits management plan**
Correct. The benefits management plan defines the benefits that are derived directly from
the project’s deliverables, how the benefits continue into the future, how the value is
maintained and improved, and who is responsible for doing that work.
- **C Stakeholder register**
Incorrect. The question states that the project manager is about to start the processes
associated with the Initiating Process Group. The stakeholder register is an output of the
Identify Stakeholders process, which is part of the Initiating Process Group. Hence, the
stakeholder register has not yet been created.
- **D Project charter**
Incorrect. The question states that the project manager is about to start the processes
associated with the Initiating Process Group. The project charter is an output of the
Develop Project Charter process, which is part of the Initiating Process Group. Hence, the
project charter has not yet been created.

**Reference:**

- **A Guide to the Project Management Body of Knowledge, (PMBOK® Guide) – Sixth Edition,**
Project Management Institute Inc., 2017, Page(s) 509
